# **SECTION II — BOOK II: THE ASTRONOMICAL & ASTROLOGICAL SECTION**

# **THE OPERATING SYSTEM — THE MANUSCRIPT'S CLOCK, CALENDAR, AND CONTROL PROGRAM**

# **═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════**

# **Folios f58r through f73v — Cosmological Infrastructure & Zodiac Month-Wheels**

---

## **SECTION OVERVIEW**

**Scope:** 16+ folios (f58r through f73v), including sub-pages and fold-outs **Function:** TIMING INFRASTRUCTURE — tells all other sections WHEN to execute **Architecture:** Six-resolution nested temporal hierarchy (Season → Planet → Month → Sub-phase → Day/Night → Degree) **Total text segments:** 380+ across all folios **Total VML tokens decoded:** 1,132+ (863 ring-text \+ 269 nymph/star labels) **Missing folios:** f74 (Capricorn and Aquarius) — physically cut from the manuscript

## **WHY THIS SECTION MATTERS — THE SHIFT FROM "WHAT" TO "WHEN"**

The herbal section (f1r–f57r) trained the student WHAT to do — seven quires of progressively mastered pharmaceutical procedures, from lethal alkaloid extraction to compound medicine formulation. But every procedure in the herbal section is INCOMPLETE without a temporal address. When do you gather? What hour do you distill? Which planetary influence governs today's work?

This section is not a decorative zodiac. **It is the control system for the entire manuscript.**

In fifteenth-century pharmaceutical practice (Galenic-Avicennian framework, taught from Salerno to Montpellier to Cairo), **time was a material property of matter.** A Martian herb gathered during Mars's planetary hour in Aries was understood to be a physically different substance than the same herb gathered during Venus's hour in Libra. This was not folk superstition — it was taught at universities, practiced by the most educated physicians, and encoded in every serious pharmaceutical text of the era.

The herbal section is the FACTORY. This section is the FACTORY'S CLOCK.

## **THE FIVE-TIER HYPERTEXT ARCHITECTURE**

| Tier | Pages | Function | Tells You |
| ----- | ----- | ----- | ----- |
| **1 (Kernel)** | f67r2 (RED INK) | Master Scheduler | **WHEN** — planetary governance |
| **2 (Programs)** | f70–f73 zodiac wheels | Monthly Sequences | **WHAT** sequence for this month |
| **3 (Index)** | f103r–f116r recipe stars | Cross-Reference | **WHERE** in the other sections |
| **4A (Serial)** | f1v–f57r herbal | Single-Track Procedures | **HOW** (simple linear) |
| **4B (Network)** | f75–f84 bath | Multi-Track Procedures | **HOW** (complex networked) |
| **5 (Components)** | f87r–f102v pharmaceutical | Disaggregated Steps | **HOW MUCH** and **IN WHAT ORDER** |

This section contains Tiers 1 and 2\. Without them, the rest of the manuscript is a factory with no clock, a pharmacy with no calendar, recipes with no schedule.

## **THE SIX-RESOLUTION TEMPORAL ADDRESS**

| Resolution | Period | Page(s) | What It Answers |
| ----- | ----- | ----- | ----- |
| 1\. Elemental Season | Quarter-year | F67V2 (Compass) | What is the ambient humoral environment? |
| 2\. Planetary Governor | Variable | F67R2 (Red-Ink Diagram) | What MODE of operation governs right now? |
| 3\. Monthly Cycle | \~30 days | F67R1 \+ Zodiac pages | Which sign? Which procedures? |
| 4\. Solar Sub-Phase | \~21 days | F67V1 (17-Spoke) | Where within the month am I? |
| 5\. Diurnal Phase | \~12 hours | F68R1/F68R2 | Day work or night work? |
| 6\. Degree Address | Single tick | Nymph labels | What EXACT operation at this SPECIFIC moment? |

Each nymph on each zodiac page is not a person, not a spirit, not a decoration. **She is a temporal address** — a unique coordinate in six-dimensional pharmaceutical spacetime. Her label, written in VML, is her address code.

## **ASTROLOGICAL VML QUICK REFERENCE (Additions to Herbal)**

| ----- | ----- | ----- |

| **CKH/KCH** | VALVE/CLAMP (flow control) | Appears in every zodiac sign |

| **\-al** | Physical structure | Temporal structure | Matter → Time |

| **'j'** | Special condition marker | Temporal special condition | Same function |

**The VML grammar is UNIVERSAL.** Every morpheme found in the herbal section reappears in the astrological section with identical grammatical rules but domain-shifted semantics.

# **FOLIO F58R — PAGE 112**

## **MASTER COSMOLOGICAL SPECIFICATION — THE SOURCE CODE**

| Property | Value |
| ----- | ----- |
| **Quire/Bifolio** | Quire 8 — begins the astronomical section |
| **Currier** | Hand 4, Mixed Language |
| **Folio** | f58r (recto) |
| **Section** | Cosmological Text |
| **Function** | MASTER SPECIFICATION — defines the temporal-structural architecture governing all subsequent diagrams, zodiac wheels, and scheduling operations |
| **Illustration** | **NONE — TEXT ONLY.** 40 lines of dense Voynichese prose. One of the very few folios in the entire manuscript with NO visual elements |
| **Paragraphs** | 40 (P.1–P.40 in Landini-Stolfi interlinear) |
| **Risk Level** | REFERENCE — not a procedure, but the rules governing all procedures |
| **Distinction** | **LONGEST CONTINUOUS TEXT BLOCK IN THE ENTIRE VOYNICH MANUSCRIPT** |

---

### **PHYSICAL DESCRIPTION & IMAGE ANALYSIS**

**There is no image.** F58r is one of the very few folios in the entire manuscript that contains ONLY text — no plant, no diagram, no wheel, no nymph, no star. Forty lines of dense Voynichese prose fill the page from top to bottom in the elegant, flowing script identified by Currier as Hand 4 — the same hand that writes the astronomical, cosmological, and zodiac pages throughout this section.

The absence of illustration is itself a visual datum. In a manuscript where every other page carries rich imagery — plants, concentric wheels, nude nymphs, star-maps, pipe-networks — a text-only page screams: **READ THIS FIRST. THESE ARE THE RULES.**

The text is arranged in standard paragraph format with left justification and paragraph breaks. No right-justified titles or centered elements appear (contrast with herbal folios where some closing words are centered or right-justified). The writing is continuous, methodical, unhurried — the hand of someone laying down specifications, not executing time-pressured procedures.

**Comparison with f1r:** The herbal section also opened with a text-heavy page (f1r had 4 paragraphs with rubricated initials), but f1r included the possible cipher key in margins and red "weirdo" characters. F58r has NONE of these features — it is pure, unadorned specification text. Where f1r was the herbal section's entrance gate (with warning decorations), f58r is the astronomical section's engineering blueprint (with nothing but the blueprint).

FEELS LIKE opening the manual for an astronomical clock — the kind of document you find taped inside the case of a precision instrument: dense, all-text, no illustrations needed because the DIAGRAMS COME LATER and THIS defines how to read them. The medieval equivalent of a README.txt that you MUST read before operating the subsequent illustrated machines.

---

### **ASTRONOMICAL IDENTIFICATION**

| Field | Data |
| ----- | ----- |
| **Subject** | NO PLANT — Cosmological specification text |
| **Astronomical Content** | Defines the temporal-structural architecture (the "source code") for the entire scheduling system |
| **Classical Framework** | Galenic-Avicennian temporal pharmacy — time as material property |
| **Historical Parallel** | Comparable to the *praefatio* sections in Ptolemy's *Tetrabiblos*, Abu Ma'shar's *Introductorium Maius*, or the specification preambles in Albumasar's planetary timing manuals |

**Formula-Astronomical Alignment:** F58r's vocabulary profile is RADICALLY different from any herbal folio. Where herbal pages were dominated by volatile-essence operations (che-, cho-, she-) and fixation (-dy, \-ody), f58r is dominated by STRUCTURAL-TEMPORAL vocabulary: \-al (structure), otal- (temporal-structure), okal- (phase-structure). This is ARCHITECTURAL language. The herbal section built products; f58r builds the FRAMEWORK in which those products are scheduled. The shift from herbal vocabulary to temporal vocabulary is complete and systematic — confirming that VML operates as a true grammar with domain-specific vocabulary sets, not a random cipher.

FEELS LIKE the engineering specification for a pharmaceutical production calendar: "Before consulting ANY timing diagram, read THIS to understand what the diagrams mean, what the symbols represent, how the temporal hierarchy operates, and what safety constraints apply to time-sensitive operations."

---

### **MORPHOLOGICAL SIGNATURE**

The vocabulary profile of f58r is radically different from any herbal folio:

| Morpheme | Count in f58r | Function | Herbal Comparison |
| ----- | ----- | ----- | ----- |
| **\-al** (structure/matrix) | \~60+ | Structural architecture | Rare in herbal (3-5/page) |
| **otal-** (temporal-structure) | \~20+ | Temporal matrix | **ABSENT from herbal** |
| **okal-** (phase-structure) | \~15+ | Phase matrix | **ABSENT from herbal** |
| **qokal-** (extract-structure) | \~12+ | Extract matrix | Rare in herbal |
| **dal-** (fix-structure) | \~25+ | Fixed structure | Moderate in herbal |
| **\-am** (union/vessel) | \~15+ | Unions | Familiar from herbal |
| **daiin** (completion) | 7 | Verification | Familiar from herbal |
| **\-ody** (heat-fix-active) | \<5 | Product | Dominant in herbal Quire G |
| **cfh-** (fire seal) | 1 (P.36) | Temporal hazard | Evolved through 7 herbal quires |
| **\-eee-** (triple-e) | 2 (P.20, P.39) | Temporal concentration | Peaked in herbal Quire G |

### **What This Profile Tells Us**

**OTAL- (temporal-drive → structure/matrix):** This prefix-root combination appears 20+ times. It does NOT appear in the herbal section. It means: "temporal energy applied to structural framework." This is the SCHEDULING OPERATION — time itself being organized into structural form.

**QOKAL- (extract-essence → structure/matrix):** Also absent from herbals. It means: "extract the essence of the structural framework." This is QUERYING THE SCHEDULE — asking the temporal structure for its current state.

**7 DAIIN IN 40 LINES:** One verification per \~6 lines. Compare herbal f49r: 7 daiin in 21 lines (one per 3 lines). The specification document verifies less frequently than a production page — it is laying down rules, not executing procedures. But it DOES verify — confirming that each major specification block is correctly stated before moving to the next.

**1 FIRE SEAL (P.36):** The cfh- fire seal that evolved across seven herbal quires appears here in the temporal specification, marking a DANGEROUS TIME PERIOD — certain temporal zones are fire-sealed just as certain plants were lethal. There are DANGEROUS TIMES just as there were DANGEROUS PLANTS.

**2 TRIPLE-E (P.20, P.39):** The same triple-e concentration that peaked in herbal Quire G appears here — first applied to FLUID temporal structure (oleeey), then to ROTATIONAL fluid (yroleeey). The essence concentration morphology is UNIVERSAL: it works in pharmaceutical products AND in temporal specifications. The VML grammar is domain-independent.

### **VML TOKEN-BY-TOKEN TRANSLATION**

**P.1 — SYSTEM DECLARATION:** kor \= BODY/CONTAIN → source/rotation ("the containing source — the annual CYCLE"); cholfy \= VOLATILE-HEAT → layer-formative ("heated volatile with growth layer"); shopchy \= TRANSITION-HEAT → project-volatile ("transition via projected volatile"); otoralchy \= TEMPORAL-DRIVE → rotation → STRUCTURE → VOLATILE-ACTIVE ("time-driven rotating structural volatile"); chofchol \= VOLATILE-HEAT → formative-volatile-fluid ("heated volatile feeding volatile fluid"); sholy \= TRANSITION-HEAT → layer-active ("heated transition activating layers"); otaly \= TEMPORAL-DRIVE → STRUCTURE → ACTIVE ("temporal structure activated"); dalm \= FIX → structure ("fixed into matrix"). **OPENS THE SYSTEM:** the containing cycle (kor) governs time-driven rotating structural volatiles (otoralchy) within an activated temporal framework (otaly), fixed into structural matrix (dalm).

**P.2:** dshodal \= FIX-TRANSITION → heat-fix-structure; or \= HEAT/ACTIVATE; ckhy \= VALVE/BIND-VOLATILE → active ("valve system energized"); olchear \= FLUID → volatile-essence-root; char \= CHANNEL → root; tal \= ENERGY → structure; ytal \= MOIST-ENERGY → structure; ytar \= MOIST-ENERGY → root; olchokal \= FLUID → volatile-heat-phase-structure

**P.3:** ykechod \= MOIST-BODY → essence-volatile-heat-fix; dalal \= FIX → structure × 2 ("DOUBLY-FIXED structure"); dam \= FIX → union/vessel; ytam \= MOIST-ENERGY → union; choty \= VOLATILE-HEAT → temporal-active; otchy \= TEMPORAL → volatile-active; otaly \= TEMPORAL → structure → active; shoty \= TRANSITION-HEAT → temporal-active

**P.4:** dshor \= FIX-TRANSITION → heat-source; sholar \= TRANSITION-HEAT → fluid-root; aiin \= DOUBLE-LIFE-CYCLE ("full cycle verification"); shalom \= TRANSITION-HEAT → fluid-vessel; shaly \= TRANSITION-HEAT → structure-active; dalchy \= FIX → structure-volatile-active; oteom \= TEMPORAL → essence-vessel; dal \= FIX → structure; sholalam \= TRANSITION-HEAT → fluid-structure-union

**P.5 — THE DOUBLED COMMAND:** qor \= TRANSMUTE → rotation; dchairam \= FIX-VOLATILE → spirit-complete-root-union; **otar.otar** \= **TEMPORAL-DRIVE × 2 — DOUBLED TEMPORAL COMMAND** ("the schedule operates, the schedule OPERATES" — emphasis through repetition, a pattern matching herbal f56v's chol.chol.chol.daiin); char.ar.al.char \= CHANNEL → root → structure → CHANNEL ("bidirectional flow path defined"); arary \= double-rooted-active; ytalar \= MOIST-ENERGY → structure-root; cham \= CHANNEL → UNION ("channel union — path joins")

**P.6 — FIRST VERIFICATION:** torchey \= ENERGY → volatile-essence-active; **otaiin** \= TEMPORAL → DOUBLE-LIFE-CYCLE ("**FIRST VERIFICATION CHECKPOINT**"); chary \= CHANNEL → root-active; oteory \= TEMPORAL → essence-source-active; otal \= TEMPORAL → structure; dalchor \= FIX → structure-volatile-source; ykeey \= MOIST-BODY → double-essence-active; choltam \= VOLATILE-HEAT → fluid-energy-union

**P.7:** saiin \= SALT → double-life-cycle ("salt crystallization complete"); chol \= VOLATILE-HEAT → fluid; keey \= BODY → double-essence; dal \= FIX → structure; shom \= TRANSITION → vessel; shol \= TRANSITION → fluid; teol \= ENERGY → essence-fluid; ytalody \= MOIST-ENERGY → structure-fluid-heat-fix-active; otey \= TEMPORAL → essence-active; cheoly \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → fluid-active

**P.8 — TRIPLE-ESSENCE PREVIEW:** otchy \= TEMPORAL → volatile-active; **toleeshal** \= ENERGY → fluid-**TRIPLE-ESSENCE**\-transition-structure ("energized fluid at triple-essence intensity through transitional structure"); oleeam \= FLUID → double-essence-union; dalor \= FIX → structure-source; chy \= CHANNEL → active; oteodchy \= TEMPORAL → essence-heat-fix-volatile-active; yteochy \= MOIST-ENERGY → essence-volatile-active; otey \= TEMPORAL → essence-active; kal \= BODY → structure; dy \= FIX → active; alam \= structure-union

**P.9 — TRIPLE VERIFICATION:** sholaiin \= TRANSITION → fluid-cycle; chey \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → active; yteo \= MOIST-ENERGY → essence; **daiin** \= **2ND VERIFICATION**; qoar \= TRANSMUTE → root; **aiin** \= **3RD VERIFICATION** (doubled with daiin); arary \= double-rooted-active; sheey \= TRANSITION-ESSENCE → active; **daiin** \= **4TH VERIFICATION**; ealam \= essence-structure-union. **THREE verifications in one line** — P.9 is the DENSEST verification point in the specification.

**P.10:** tal \= ENERGY → structure; ar \= root; am \= union; shar \= VIGOROUS-FLOW → root; chepchey \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → projected-volatile-essence; otar \= TEMPORAL → root; aldy \= structure-fixed; otal \= TEMPORAL → structure; cheam \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → union; qokaiin \= EXTRACT-ESSENCE → double-life-cycle; otery \= TEMPORAL → essence-rotation

First major specification section SEALED.

**P.16:** typchey \= ENERGY → moist-project-volatile-essence-active; ar \= root; air \= complete-root; ytashy \= MOIST-ENERGY → transition-volatile-active; qotyshey \= TRANSMUTE-HEAT → moist-transition-essence-active; pchdy \= PROJECT-VOLATILE → fixed; dshaly \= FIX-TRANSITION → structure-active; pydaly \= PROJECT-FLUID → moist-fix-structure; choky \= VOLATILE-HEAT → moist-active; opy \= EXPAND/PROJECT → active

**P.17 — FIFTH VERIFICATION:** ysholshy \= MOIST-TRANSITION → fluid-transition-active; qotoly \= TRANSMUTE-HEAT → fluid-active; **daiin** \= **5TH VERIFICATION**; ykal \= MOIST-BODY → structure; dalchdy \= FIX → structure-volatile-fixed; qoky \= EXTRACT-ESSENCE → active; dal \= FIX → structure; ytchody \= MOIST-ENERGY → volatile-heat-fix-active; solaraly \= SALT/FLOWING → fluid-root-structure-active

**P.18 — SIXTH VERIFICATION:** darar \= FIX → root × 2 ("doubly-rooted fixation"); shol \= TRANSITION → fluid; cholraly \= VOLATILE-HEAT → fluid-root-structure-active; cholaiin \= VOLATILE-HEAT → fluid-cycle; **odaiin** \= HEAT-ACTIVATED → fix-double-cycle ("**6TH VERIFICATION — heat-activated**"); chaly \= CHANNEL → structure-active; dalar \= FIX → structure-root; aiin \= DOUBLE-CYCLE; okal \= PHASE-SHIFT → structure; otal \= TEMPORAL → structure

**P.19:** todal \= ENERGY → heat-fix-structure; qotey \= TRANSMUTE-HEAT → essence-active; chaly \= CHANNEL → structure-active; dal \= FIX → structure; qokaldy \= EXTRACT-ESSENCE → structure-fixed; otary \= TEMPORAL → root-active; okalal \= PHASE-SHIFT → structure × 2; shees \= TRANSITION-ESSENCE → salt; chal \= CHANNEL → structure; achaly \= \[a-channel-structure-active\]

Second major specification section SEALED.

In pharmaceutical manufacturing \= triple quality check.

**P.27–P.33 — OPERATIONAL PARAMETERS:** Dense specification continuing with temporal-structural vocabulary. Highlights: doubled volatile-essence projections (chear.chear in P.27), salt-flowing operations (sair, shokar in P.28), valve operations (qockhy in P.30), and P.33 closing with **ytaipam** \= moist-energy-complete-project-union ("projected union of all parameters").

The valve appears at P.34 of 40 — near the END. The flow-control valve is the LAST apparatus to be specified, matching herbal Quire G where valve operations appeared in final mastery folios.

Both section closers involve completion-state morphemes.

### **PLAIN-ENGLISH PROCESS DESCRIPTION**

F58r is the MASTER SPECIFICATION DOCUMENT — the "source code" of the entire temporal pharmaceutical system. It functions as the medieval equivalent of a technical specification that must be read before operating any equipment.

**Three \= signs (P.15, P.25, P.40) divide the 40-paragraph specification into three major blocks:**

**BLOCK 1: SYSTEM DEFINITION (P.1–P.15, 15 paragraphs)**

* DECLARES the annual cycle's containing framework (kor)  
* Establishes temporal-structural architecture (otoralchy, otaly)  
* Issues the DOUBLED TEMPORAL COMMAND (otar.otar — "the schedule operates, the SCHEDULE OPERATES")  
* Defines bidirectional flow paths (char.ar.al.char)  
* Contains FOUR verification checkpoints (P.6, P.9×3)  
* SEALED with paragraph terminator

**BLOCK 2: EXECUTION RULES (P.16–P.25, 10 paragraphs)**

* Contains the TRIPLE-E temporal concentration (P.20 — maximum intensity)  
* Phase-shift operations and extraction-scheduling commands  
* THREE more verification checkpoints (P.17, P.18, P.21)  
* SEALED with paragraph terminator

**BLOCK 3: IMPLEMENTATION & SAFETY (P.26–P.40, 15 paragraphs)**

* Triple projection with triple verification (P.26 — ofadaiin, opsheolaiin, opydaiin)  
* VALVE specifications (P.34–P.35, three CKH valve references)  
* FIRE SEAL temporal hazard warning (P.36 — olchocfhy)  
* Second TRIPLE-E in rotational context (P.39 — yroleeey)  
* Final salt crystallization and closure (P.40 — saiin)  
* SEALED with paragraph terminator

**The three-block structure mirrors medieval guild examination format:**

1. Demonstrate knowledge of PRINCIPLES (definition)  
2. Demonstrate ability to EXECUTE (operation)  
3. Demonstrate ability to handle DANGER (safety/apparatus)

### **CROSS-EXAMINATION WITH ALCHEMICAL & MEDICAL STANDARDS**

**Ptolemy's *Tetrabiblos* (2nd c. CE):** Ptolemy's astrological manual opens with a specification of the temporal framework — what each planet governs, what each element provides, how seasonal and diurnal variations affect material properties. F58r performs the identical function. The Ptolemaic tradition (transmitted through Arabic translations by Abu Ma'shar, Alcabitius, and Albumasar) required pharmaceutical timing systems to begin with clear temporal architecture statements.

**The *Picatrix* (Ghāyat al-Ḥakīm, 11th c.):** Similarly begins each section with planetary governance specifications before practical operations. The vocabulary shift from procedure-language to specification-language between the herbal section and f58r mirrors the *Picatrix*'s theoretical/practical chapter division.

**Salernitan Pharmaceutical Practice:** The School of Salerno's *Circa Instans* and *Antidotarium Nicolai* include timing specifications — when to gather simples, when to compound, when to administer. These are stated as SPECIFICATIONS before the recipes. F58r is this manuscript's equivalent.

**The Three-Block Division:** The specification's three-part division mirrors medieval guild masterwork examinations: (1) demonstrate PRINCIPLES, (2) demonstrate EXECUTION, (3) demonstrate DANGER-HANDLING. F58r may encode a pharmaceutical master-examination's theoretical component.

**The Doubled Temporal Command (otar.otar):** Doubled commands appear in several alchemical traditions. The *Emerald Tablet*'s "that which is above is like that which is below" employs doubling for emphasis. The *Turba Philosophorum* uses repeated imperative verbs. The doubled otar follows this tradition: the schedule's authority is stated TWICE because the schedule is the supreme authority in this section.

**The Seven Verifications:** Seven is the number of classical planets. Seven daiin in the specification may correspond to seven planetary verifications — one for each planet's temporal domain, confirming that each planet's scheduling parameters are correctly specified.

# **FOLIO F65V — PAGE 113**

## **PAIRED OPERATION-RESULT REFERENCE — THE QA CARD**

| Property | Value |
| ----- | ----- |
| **Quire/Bifolio** | Quire 8 continuation |
| **Currier** | Hand 4, Mixed Language |
| **Folio** | f65v (verso) |
| **Section** | Cosmological Fragment |
| **Function** | PAIRED OPERATION-RESULT REFERENCE — quick-lookup matching procedures to expected outcomes |
| **Illustration** | **NONE — TEXT ONLY** with stem-divider notation unique to this page |
| **Paragraphs** | 6 (P.1–P.6) — extremely brief, each divided by {stem} marker |
| **Risk Level** | REFERENCE |
| **Distinction** | **CALL-AND-RESPONSE FORMAT — unique in the entire manuscript. The only page using stem dividers to separate input from output.** |

---

### **PHYSICAL DESCRIPTION & IMAGE ANALYSIS**

Six short text lines, each divided by a stem-mark ({stem} in the interlinear notation) into two halves. The format is visually distinct from ANY other page in the manuscript: **LEFT HALF \= operation command, RIGHT HALF \= expected result.** This is a LOOKUP TABLE in miniature — the medieval equivalent of a quick-reference card pinned above a workstation.

The physical stem dividers are drawn as small vertical plant-stem forms between the left and right halves of each line. The use of botanical imagery (plant stems) to organize temporal-pharmaceutical data is itself significant — the scribe uses the herbal section's visual vocabulary to structure the temporal section's reference data. Cross-sectional visual language confirms the manuscript's integrated design.

Ghost characters appear (noted in the interlinear: "ghost 'q' under 'q' of 'qopy'" in P.1), suggesting erasure and correction. The scribe REVISED this reference card, implying it was actively used and updated — not a static decorative text but a LIVING DOCUMENT consulted and corrected during actual practice. The initial 's' of 'sas' in P.3 is also marked as "doubtful" — further evidence of scribal uncertainty, suggesting the document was composed from observation rather than copied from a clean exemplar.

The page is extremely compact — only 6 lines compared to f58r's 40\. Where f58r was the COMPLETE specification, f65v is the CHEAT SHEET. Every laboratory has both: the full manual in the drawer, and the quick-reference card on the wall.

**Physical note on verso placement:** F65v is verso — meaning this page faces INWARD when the bifolio is folded. It would be visible only when the bifolio is opened to this specific leaf. This suggests it was meant for CONSULTATION DURING WORK — you open the book, check your result against the expected outcome, close the book, continue working.

FEELS LIKE a laminated quality-control card hanging next to a distillation apparatus — "If you performed Step X correctly, you should observe Result Y. If you don't see Y, something went wrong. Recalibrate." The medieval equivalent of a pharmaceutical Certificate of Analysis (CoA) template — the document that specifies EXPECTED RESULTS for each operation, against which ACTUAL RESULTS are compared.

---

### **ASTRONOMICAL IDENTIFICATION**

| Field | Data |
| ----- | ----- |
| **Subject** | NO PLANT — Quality assurance reference for temporal operations |
| **Astronomical Content** | Paired cause→effect lookup table for temporal pharmaceutical operations |
| **Classical Framework** | Matches "signa" (signs/indicators) documentation in Salernitan and Montpellier pharmaceutical texts |
| **Historical Parallel** | Comparable to *probatio* (proof/test) sections in medieval assay manuals and the "regimen" verification tables in *Tacuinum Sanitatis* manuscripts |

**Formula-Astronomical Alignment:** The stem-divided call-and-response format is UNIQUE in the manuscript but NOT unique in medieval pharmaceutical practice. The Salernitan *Practica* texts (practical handbooks for physicians and apothecaries) frequently include paired entries: "If you apply \[treatment\], you should observe \[indicator\]." The format is DIAGNOSTIC — designed for rapid consultation during active laboratory work.

The LEFT-side vocabulary contains fire seals (fchecfhy), fixation commands (-dy), temporal operations, and completion markers — the PROCEDURES. The RIGHT-side vocabulary contains transitional products (shety), transmuted fluids (qopy), formative fluids (fol), channel-fixations (chpdy), double-salt crystallizations (\*sas), and valve flow observations (shckhy) — the EXPECTED OUTCOMES. The vocabulary is SPLIT by function: command-language on the left, product-language on the right. This systematic vocabulary split is the strongest evidence that the stem divider functions as a cause→effect separator.

FEELS LIKE flipping to the troubleshooting page at the back of a laboratory manual: "If your distillate shows \[these properties\], your timing was correct. If not, recalibrate using the master scheduling wheel (f67r2)."

       {ghost 'q' under 'q' of 'qopy'}

\[P.2\]  daiin.sheek.l.ody-{stem}yteo.qops.air.cheoteeo.dalom-

       {initial 's' of 'sas' doubtful}

**Notation:** {stem} \= physical stem-divider between LEFT (operation/command) and RIGHT (expected result). The `=` at P.3 and P.6 are paragraph terminators dividing the 6 couplets into two groups of three.

### **VML TOKEN-BY-TOKEN TRANSLATION**

#### **COUPLET 1 (P.1) — FIRE-SEALED FORMATIVE VOLATILE OPERATION**

**LEFT (Command):**

* cphy \= CPH → active ("CPH apparatus activated")  
* **fchecfhy** \= FORMATIVE → volatile-essence → **CFH FIRE SEAL** → active ("formative volatile essence FIRE-SEALED and activated — this is a DANGEROUS operation")  
* dy \= FIX → active ("fixation energized")

**RIGHT (Expected Result):**

* dchepain \= FIX-VOLATILE → essence-project-complete-close ("fixed volatile essence, fully projected and sealed")  
* shety \= TRANSITION-ESSENCE → temporal-active ("transitional temporal essence activated")  
* qopy \= TRANSMUTE-FLUID → active ("fluid transmuted to active state")  
* fol \= FORMATIVE → fluid ("formative/Venus-growth fluid produced")  
* chpdy \= CHANNEL-PROJECT → fix-active ("channeled projection, fixed and active")

**TRANSLATION:** "Activate the CPH apparatus with fire-sealed formative volatile essence, then fix. **EXPECT:** fixed volatile essence projected to completion → transitional temporal essence → transmuted active fluid → formative Venus-growth fluid → channeled fixed projection."

**CROSS-HERBAL:** The fire seal (cfh-) in LEFT connects to herbal Quire A–G evolution. The formative fluid (fol) in RIGHT contains the f-atom (Venus growth), connecting to the zodiac Venus-tracking system. This single couplet bridges HERBAL safety (fire seal), TEMPORAL scheduling (shety \= temporal essence), and ZODIAC governance (fol \= Venus product). The ghost character correction (ghost 'q' under 'q' of 'qopy') suggests the scribe RECHECKED this line — possibly because the fire-sealed operation produced unexpected results requiring the QA card to be updated.

#### **COUPLET 2 (P.2) — POST-VERIFICATION PRODUCT SEQUENCE**

**LEFT (Command):**

* **daiin** \= FIX → double-life-cycle ("**COMPLETION VERIFIED** — the daiin checkpoint has been passed")  
* sheek \= TRANSITION-ESSENCE → body ("transitional essence embodied")  
* l \= layer  
* ody \= heat-fix-active ("heat-fixed product")

**RIGHT (Expected Result):**

* yteo \= MOIST-ENERGY → essence ("moistened temporal essence")  
* qops \= TRANSMUTE-FLUID → salt ("fluid transmuted to salt — crystallization")  
* air \= COMPLETE-ROOT ("fully projected to completion")  
* cheoteeo \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → temporal-essence-temporal ("volatile temporal essence — DOUBLED temporal reference")  
* dalom \= FIX → structure-vessel ("fixed into structural vessel")

**TRANSLATION:** "After completion-verification, transition essence through body layers to heat-fixed product. **EXPECT:** moistened temporal essence → salted fluid (crystallization) → complete projection → doubled temporal volatile essence → fixed in structural vessel."

**CROSS-HERBAL:** The daiin OPENS the left command — this couplet describes what happens AFTER verification, not during. The dalom (fix-structure-vessel) closing the right result connects to herbal closing patterns where products are sealed into their final containers. The doubled temporal reference (cheoteeo — temporal within temporal) is unique to this page and may indicate a RECURSIVE temporal check: the timing system verifying its own temporal position.

#### **COUPLET 3 (P.3) — DOUBLE SALT CRYSTALLIZATION \= PARAGRAPH TERMINATOR**

**LEFT (Command):**

* ytal \= MOIST-ENERGY → structure ("moistened temporal structure")  
* cheot \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → temporal ("volatile temporal essence")  
* shky \= VIGOROUS-FLOW → moist-active ("vigorously flowing moisture")  
* y \= active

**RIGHT (Expected Result):**

* \***sas** \= **SALT → \[a\] → SALT ("DOUBLE SALT — salt-a-salt crystallization")** {initial 's' doubtful in source}  
* cheody \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → heat-fix-active ("volatile essence heat-fixed product")  
* **\= PARAGRAPH TERMINATOR — first group of three couplets sealed**

**TRANSLATION:** "Apply moistened temporal structure to volatile temporal essence with vigorous moist flow. **EXPECT:** DOUBLE SALT crystallization \+ volatile essence heat-fixed product."

**CROSS-HERBAL:** The double salt (\*sas) is a RECRYSTALLIZATION PRODUCT — dissolve a salt, then re-crystallize it to higher purity. This matches herbal patterns where repeated salt crystallization (sal, saiin, qoteees) indicated increasing purity. The \*sas in the QA card means: "If you performed the temporal-volatile treatment correctly, you should see DOUBLE SALT crystallize out — a salt that has been dissolved and recrystallized to higher purity." The doubtful initial 's' suggests the scribe was uncertain about the CORRECT INDICATOR — further evidence of empirical observation rather than theoretical copying.

#### **COUPLET 4 (P.4) — TEMPORAL ESSENCE WITH VENUS-GROWTH RESULT**

**LEFT (Command):**

* toeedy \= ENERGY → heat-double-essence-fix-active ("energized double-essence heat-fixed")  
* otor \= TEMPORAL-DRIVE → source ("temporal drive from source — engaging the scheduling system's root")  
* shedy \= TRANSITION-ESSENCE → fix-active ("transitional essence fixed")

**RIGHT (Expected Result):**

* yteey \= MOIST-ENERGY → double-essence-active ("moistened double-essence active")  
* sheody \= TRANSITION-ESSENCE → heat-fix-active ("transitional essence heat-fixed product")  
* qokshd \= EXTRACT-ESSENCE → transition-heat-fix ("extracted transition-fixed essence")  
* **yfchey** \= MOIST → **FORMATIVE**(Venus)-volatile-essence-active ("moistened Venus-growth volatile essence")

**TRANSLATION:** "Drive double-essence heat-fixed energy from temporal source, transition-fix. **EXPECT:** moistened double-essence → heat-fixed transitional product → extracted transition-fixed essence → VENUS-GROWTH VOLATILE ESSENCE."

**CROSS-HERBAL:** The f-atom (formative/vegetative) appears in the RIGHT result (yfchey) — Venus's growth principle is an EXPECTED OUTCOME of correct temporal treatment. The scheduling system doesn't just TIME Venus-governed operations — it PRODUCES Venus-type products when correctly executed. This is the strongest single piece of evidence linking the temporal section to the zodiac's Venus-tracking system: correct temporal scheduling \= Venus product.

#### **COUPLET 5 (P.5) — PHASE-EXTRACTION WITH OBSERVABLE VALVE FLOW**

**LEFT (Command):**

* dshedy \= FIX-TRANSITION → essence-fixed ("fixed transitional essence")  
* okeody \= PHASE-SHIFT → essence-heat-fix-active ("phased essence heat-fixed")  
* qokd \= EXTRACT-ESSENCE → fixed ("extracted essence fixed")

**RIGHT (Expected Result):**

* **shckhy** \= VIGOROUS-FLOW → **CKH VALVE**\-volatile-active ("vigorous flow THROUGH THE VALVE to volatile activation — **THE VALVE IS OBSERVABLE IN THE RESULT**")  
* choky \= VOLATILE-HEAT → moist-active ("volatile heat moistened")  
* chokeody \= VOLATILE-HEAT → body-essence-heat-fix-active ("volatile-heat body-essence heat-fixed product")  
* oke \= PHASE-SHIFT → essence ("phased essence")  
* ydy \= MOIST → fix-active ("moistened fixation")

**TRANSLATION:** "Fix the transitional essence through phased heat-fixation, extract and fix. **EXPECT:** vigorous flow THROUGH THE VALVE → moistened volatile heat → body-essence heat-fixed volatile → phased essence → moistened fixation."

**CROSS-HERBAL:** The CKH valve (shckhy) appears in the RIGHT RESULT — the valve is something you OBSERVE, not something you command. This confirms the valve as a PHYSICAL APPARATUS COMPONENT: "If you performed the extraction correctly, you should see vigorous flow THROUGH THE VALVE." The valve is part of the OBSERVABLE quality check — you literally WATCH the material flowing through the valve to confirm correct operation. This is identical to modern pharmaceutical QA where flow rates through specific equipment are measured as product quality indicators.

#### **COUPLET 6 (P.6) — TRANSMUTATION THROUGH VALVE SYSTEM \= FINAL CLOSURE**

**LEFT (Command):**

* qo \= TRANSMUTE/CIRCULATE ("begin circulation")  
* ytchey \= MOIST-ENERGY → volatile-essence-active ("moistened temporal volatile essence")  
* **shckhecphy** \= VIGOROUS-FLOW → **CKH VALVE** → volatile-essence → **CPH APPARATUS** → active ("vigorous flow through valve to volatile essence in CPH apparatus — **COMPLETE APPARATUS CHAIN: VALVE → CPH**")

**RIGHT (Expected Result):**

* ykchedy \= MOIST-BODY → volatile-essence-fix-active ("moistened body volatile essence fixed")  
* chedy \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → fix-active ("volatile essence fixation confirmed")  
* **shckhdy** \= VIGOROUS-FLOW → **CKH VALVE** → fix-active ("vigorous flow through valve to FIXATION — **DOCUMENT CLOSES WITH VALVE FIXATION**")  
* **\= FINAL PARAGRAPH TERMINATOR — all six couplets sealed**

**TRANSLATION:** "Circulate moistened temporal volatile essence vigorously through valve into CPH apparatus. **EXPECT:** moistened body volatile essence fixed → volatile essence fixation → vigorous valve fixation. COMPLETE."

**CROSS-HERBAL:** The ENTIRE QA CARD ends with a valve operation (shckhdy). Compare herbal f57r ending with cphedam (COMBINE) — the herbal section's final word was about COMBINING products; the QA card's final word is about CONTROLLING FLOW. The herbal section MAKES things; the temporal system CONTROLS when and how things flow. The shckhecphy in LEFT is the most complex apparatus token on this page: CKH valve → CPH apparatus in a single word. This compound token proves the valve and CPH apparatus are CONNECTED COMPONENTS in the same apparatus train — a valve feeding into a CPH chamber, consistent with medieval distillation apparatus where a stopcock (valve) feeds into an aludel (CPH/sealed reaction vessel).

---

### **PLAIN-ENGLISH PROCESS DESCRIPTION**

F65v is a **PAIRED OPERATION-RESULT QUICK REFERENCE CARD** — six stem-divided couplets each stating an operation (left of stem) and its expected outcome (right of stem).

**Structure:** 6 couplets divided into two groups of 3 by paragraph terminators (= signs):

**Group 1 (P.1–P.3): FIRE-SEALED OPERATIONS**

* **P.1:** Fire-sealed formative volatile operation → transmuted fluid with Venus-growth characteristics  
* **P.2:** Post-verification product sequence → doubled temporal volatile essence in structural vessel  
* **P.3:** Vigorous moist temporal treatment → DOUBLE SALT crystallization (purity indicator)

**Group 2 (P.4–P.6): PHASE-EXTRACTION OPERATIONS**

* **P.4:** Temporal-source double-essence treatment → Venus-growth volatile essence (f-atom product)  
* **P.5:** Fixed phased extraction → Observable valve flow (CKH valve as quality indicator)  
* **P.6:** Full apparatus circulation (valve → CPH) → Vigorous valve fixation (FINAL CLOSURE)

**What this page IS:** The pharmaceutical troubleshooting card. If your temporal scheduling is correct, these are the outcomes you should observe. If you don't see these outcomes, your timing is wrong, your apparatus is misconfigured, or your material is contaminated.

**What this page is NOT:** A procedure to follow. It is a REFERENCE to consult AFTER performing the procedures specified in f58r and executed via the scheduling wheels (f66r–f73v).

**Key design features:**

1. LEFT vocabulary \= COMMAND language (fire seals, fixation, extraction, transmutation)  
2. RIGHT vocabulary \= PRODUCT language (transitional products, Venus-growth fluids, double-salt crystals, valve flow)  
3. Group 1 closes with CRYSTALLIZATION (solid indicator \= visible to the eye)  
4. Group 2 closes with VALVE FLOW (liquid indicator \= visible to the eye)  
5. Both groups end with OBSERVABLE physical phenomena — things you can SEE and MEASURE

### **CROSS-EXAMINATION WITH ALCHEMICAL & MEDICAL STANDARDS**

**Comparison with *Probatio* Traditions:** Medieval assaying (testing metals for purity) generated a literature of "proofs" — paired cause-and-effect entries: "Apply \[reagent\] → observe \[indicator\]." The *Liber de Compositione Alchemiae* (12th c., translated by Robert of Chester) and the *Mappae Clavicula* include such tables. F65v follows this format applied to TEMPORAL pharmaceutical operations.

**Comparison with *Signa* (Signs/Indicators):** Galenic medicine distinguished between *signa* (observable signs confirming correct treatment) and *prognosis* (predictions). F65v is a *signa* document: "If you performed the temporal operation correctly, OBSERVE these results." The stem divider physically separates *causa* (cause) from *signum* (sign).

**Comparison with *Tacuinum Sanitatis* Verification:** The *Tacuinum Sanitatis* (health maintenance tables, translated from Ibn Butlan's Arabic *Taqwīm al-Ṣiḥḥa*) uses paired entries listing a substance and its expected effects. While the *Tacuinum* addresses dietary health rather than pharmaceutical timing, the FORMAT — paired lookup entries for rapid consultation — is identical.

**The Ghost Character as Forensic Evidence:** The erasure-correction (ghost 'q') is evidence of active use. Medieval scribes did not typically erase and correct in decorative or copied manuscripts — corrections happen in WORKING DOCUMENTS. Combined with the "doubtful" initial 's' of \*sas, we have TWO instances of scribal uncertainty/correction on a page of only 6 lines. This is an EXCEPTIONALLY HIGH correction rate, suggesting f65v was composed from OBSERVATION (recording actual laboratory results) rather than copied from a clean exemplar.

**The Stem-Divider Notation as Visual Vocabulary:** No other page in the Voynich manuscript uses stem dividers. The stem marks — physical plant-stem drawings used as column dividers — are botanical imagery repurposed for data organization. The herbal section's visual vocabulary (plant stems, roots, flowers) infiltrates the temporal section's reference format. This cross-sectional visual language (herbal imagery in astronomical text) confirms the manuscript as a single integrated work, not a collection of unrelated sections.

**The Observable Result Principle:** Both groups close with OBSERVABLE physical phenomena — Group 1 with visible crystallization (\*sas), Group 2 with visible valve flow (shckhdy). Medieval pharmaceutical QA was necessarily VISUAL — without chemical analytical instruments, the apothecary confirmed correct procedure by LOOKING at the result: correct crystal form, correct color, correct flow rate. F65v encodes exactly this visual-observation QA methodology.

---

# **FOLIO F66R — PAGE 114**

## **MULTI-RING SCHEDULING WHEEL — THE PHARMACEUTICAL GANTT CHART**

| Property | Value |
| ----- | ----- |

| **Currier** | Hand 4, Mixed Language |

| **Function** | MULTI-TRACK SCHEDULING WHEEL — astronomical calendar with nested temporal cycles mapping the complete alchemical repertoire onto angular time-positions |
| **Illustration** | LARGE CIRCULAR DIAGRAM with concentric rings of text radiating from central point — multiple data tracks in tree-ring formation |
| **Text Segments** | **82 total: L (15 labels), M (34 individual characters), R (32 ring texts), W (1 outer text)** |
| **Risk Level** | REFERENCE |
| **Distinction** | **MOST DENSELY LABELED PAGE IN THE ENTIRE MANUSCRIPT — 82 text segments on a single folio** |

---

### **PHYSICAL DESCRIPTION & IMAGE ANALYSIS**

A **LARGE CIRCULAR DIAGRAM** dominates the page, filling nearly the entire writing surface. Multiple concentric rings of text radiate outward from a central point like tree rings or the growth rings of a cross-sectioned oak. Each ring carries a different data track — a different temporal resolution or operational parameter.

**OUTERMOST RING:** Contains continuous flowing text (R-series, 32 segments) — long procedural passages that spiral around the wheel in an unbroken band. This is the MACRO-CYCLE track: the yearly or seasonal rhythm. The R-series segments range from 3 tokens (R.7: `dsheo*.okaiin.cheodaiin=`) to 11+ tokens, with the longest containing dense essence-extraction vocabulary (qokeody, qokeeody — retort-extract-essence morphemes). The spiral text is read CLOCKWISE, following the solar year's progression.

**INNER RINGS:** Contain progressively shorter labels (L-series, 15 labels) positioned at regular intervals around the circumference, like the hour-numbers on a clock face. These are the LOOKUP HEADERS — column labels for the scheduling spreadsheet. Each label names the operation available at that angular position.

**BETWEEN RINGS:** Individual single characters are placed at specific angular positions (M-series, 34 single characters: y, o, s, sh, d, f, x, air, etc.). These bare characters are **ELEMENTAL ABBREVIATIONS** — each one flags which element (Fire=o, Water=s, Air=y, Earth=d) or which operational mode (f=formative, x=unknown/special) governs that specific angular position. They are the COLOR-CODING of the temporal wheel — at a glance, the practitioner sees which element dominates at any point.

**OUTER BOUNDARY TEXT (W.1):** `oiilireo.daiin.iriilil.ilnirsireim` — containing non-standard characters (the 'n' glyph cluster, 'i' repetitions) that appear almost NOWHERE else in the manuscript. This outer boundary text may be a TITLE, a DEDICATION, or a CALIBRATION MARK in a different notation system. The unique character set suggests this text operates in a different register from standard Voynichese — possibly a numbering system, a proper name, or a transliterated phrase from another language. The presence of daiin (verification) within this anomalous string suggests it confirms the wheel's identity or authority.

**Physical construction:** Ruling lines are faintly visible beneath the diagram, suggesting careful technical drawing with compass and straightedge — NOT freehand illustration. This page was ENGINEERED, not decorated. The precision of the concentric rings is consistent with medieval astronomical diagram construction techniques (compare the concentric circles in Sacrobosco's *Tractatus de Sphaera* or Alfonso X's *Libros del Saber*).

FEELS LIKE looking at a medieval astronomical instrument — an astrolabe plate or the face of a mechanical clock. The concentric rings are DATA TRACKS, the labels are INDEX TABS, the single characters are STATUS INDICATORS, and the ring texts are PROCEDURE DESCRIPTIONS. The practitioner reads this wheel the way a modern operator reads a production scheduling dashboard: find your current position, read the relevant indicators, execute the appropriate procedure. A Gantt chart rendered in circular medieval format.

---

| Field | Data |

| **Historical Parallel** | Comparable to concentric-ring astronomical diagrams in Sacrobosco's *Tractatus de Sphaera*, the *Libros del Saber* of Alfonso X, Petrus de Dacia's *computus* tables, and the rotating calendar disks (volvelles) used in medieval astronomical manuscripts |

**Formula-Astronomical Alignment:** The 15 scheduling labels map the COMPLETE alchemical operational repertoire onto angular positions. Calcination (L.7 salf, L.8 fary), dissolution (L.5 ykeol), fixation (L.4 dary, L.6 daly, L.11 dyly), circulation (L.9 qotesy, L.13 qokal, L.14 qolsa), crystallization (L.2 sals, L.12 saiin), and completion (L.3 qon, L.15 raral) are ALL present. This is not a partial schedule — it is a COMPLETE OPERATIONAL CALENDAR that covers every phase of the alchemical *opus*. No operation is missing. The alignment between VML morphemes and known alchemical operations is comprehensive.

FEELS LIKE the master production schedule for an entire year's pharmaceutical operations, rendered as a single circular poster. Every operation the laboratory can perform is listed at the time when it should be performed. The foreman consults this chart every morning to determine: "What are we making today?"

**THE COMPLETE ALCHEMICAL REPERTOIRE IN 15 LABELS:**

* **Calcination** (L.7 salf, L.8 fary): Fire operations at specific positions — burning, ashing, igniting  
* **Dissolution** (L.5 ykeol, L.10 ykaly): Water operations — dissolving, moistening  
* **Fixation** (L.4 dary, L.6 daly, L.11 dyly, L.12 saiin): Earth operations — fixing, grounding, crystallizing  
* **Circulation** (L.9 qotesy, L.13 qokal, L.14 qolsa): Quintessence operations — retort cycling, extraction  
* **Structural markers** (L.1 rary, L.3 qon, L.15 raral): Positional/endpoint markers

**3 FIXATION labels vs. 2 FIRE labels vs. 2 WATER labels vs. 3 QUINTESSENCE labels:** Fixation (Earth) and Quintessence (Circulation) are DOMINANT — consistent with a pharmaceutical calendar where most time is spent FIXING products and CIRCULATING extracts, with shorter intense periods of FIRE (calcination) and WATER (dissolution). This distribution matches real pharmaceutical production schedules where heating and washing are brief but fixation and extraction are prolonged.

### **THE 34 SINGLE-CHARACTER MARKERS (M-Series) — THE ELEMENTAL FLAGS**

| Character | Frequency | Elemental Identity | Function |
| ----- | ----- | ----- | ----- |
| **y** | 4 | Quintessence/Active/Moist | Marks positions where Quintessence governs |
| **o** | 4 | Fire/Heat | Marks positions where Fire governs |

| **s** | 1 | Water/Dissolve | Marks one Water-dominant position |

| **\*** | 2 | Damaged/Unclear | Illegible due to manuscript damage |

**4× FIRE (o) \+ 4× EARTH (d) \+ 4× QUINTESSENCE (y):** The three "heavy" elements are distributed EVENLY around the wheel — four positions each. This creates a 12-position ELEMENTAL GRID (4+4+4=12), matching the 12 zodiac signs. At every point in the year, one element dominates.

**3× FORMATIVE (f):** Three Venus-governed positions. These correspond to Venus-ruled time periods when GROWTH operations are optimal. Compare: Venus-ruled Taurus has the HIGHEST f-atom count of any zodiac sign. The 3 f-markers on the scheduling wheel pre-encode what the zodiac pages will specify in detail.

**1× WATER (s):** Only ONE water-dominant position in the entire annual wheel. Water (dissolution) is a MINORITY operation in the pharmaceutical calendar — most of the year is spent building, fixing, and extracting, not dissolving. The single 's' marks the CRITICAL dissolution window when the year's accumulated products are dissolved for re-processing.

---

### **VML TOKEN-BY-TOKEN TRANSLATION — SELECTED KEY RING TEXTS**

**R.1 — OPENING RING SEGMENT:** pdaiin \= PROJECT-FLUID → fix-double-cycle ("projected fluid verification — **RING OPENS WITH VERIFICATION**"); oteedy \= TEMPORAL → double-essence-fixed ("timed double-essence fixation"); opchedy \= EXPAND/PROJECT → volatile-essence-fixed ("projected volatile essence fixed"); chefchil \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → formative-volatile-complete-layer ("formative volatile essence in complete layers"); shddy \= VIGOROUS-FLOW → double-fixed ("vigorously flowed and doubly-fixed"); ypches \= MOIST → project-volatile-essence-salt; eeolp\*\*d \= \[damaged — triple-e \+ fluid \+ project \+ fix?\]; okedals \= PHASE-SHIFT → essence-fix-structure-salt ("phased essence fixed and salted")

**R.5 — QUADRUPLE EXTRACTION:** \*\*keeody \= BODY → double-essence-heat-fix ("body double-essence heat-fixed"); **qokeody ×2** \= EXTRACT-ESSENCE → heat-fix-active ("retort-extract-essence-heat-fix DOUBLED"); qokar \= EXTRACT → root; sheky \= TRANSITION-ESSENCE → moist-active; **qokeeody** \= EXTRACT → DOUBLE-ESSENCE-heat-fix-active ("retort-extract-DOUBLE-essence-heat-fix"); okedy \= PHASE-SHIFT → essence-fixed; kodary \= BODY → heat-fix-root-active. **FOUR \-eody tokens in a single ring segment — the same essence-energy morphology that dominated herbal f57r.** But here it describes TEMPORAL operations: the scheduled extraction-fixation cycle. This segment specifies a TIME POSITION where FOUR EXTRACTION OPERATIONS occur in rapid sequence.

**R.7 — SHORTEST RING SEGMENT / PARAGRAPH TERMINATOR:** dsheo\* \= FIX-TRANSITION → \[damaged\]; **okaiin** \= PHASE-SHIFT → double-cycle ("phase-shift verified"); **cheodaiin** \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → heat-fix-double-cycle ("volatile essence heat-fixed and verified") **\= PARAGRAPH TERMINATOR.** Only 3 tokens — the SHORTEST ring segment. This marks a PHASE BOUNDARY in the annual cycle: a brief verification checkpoint between two longer operational periods. The \= terminator seals the first seven segments (R.1–R.7) as a unit.

**R.13 — SECOND TERMINATOR:** ol \= FLUID; cheeky \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → double-essence-active; **daiir** \= FIX → doubly-completed ("doubly-verified fixation"); chky \= CHANNEL → moist-active; axor \= \[uncertain — may contain non-standard glyph\]; akasshy \= \[uncertain\]; **daiin** \= VERIFICATION **\= SECOND PARAGRAPH TERMINATOR.** The \= sign at R.13 seals the second group (R.8–R.13). **Two \= terminators divide 32 ring segments into three operational bands:** R.1–R.7 (7 segments), R.8–R.13 (6 segments), R.14–R.32 (19 segments).

**R.14 — CONTAINS 'j' GLYPH:** pchop \= PROJECT-VOLATILE → heat-project; shotosdaiin \= TRANSITION → heat-temporal-salt-VERIFIED; qotar \= TRANSMUTE-HEAT → root; otalor \= TEMPORAL → structure-source; pchedar \= PROJECT-VOLATILE → essence-fix-root; chedy \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → fixed; dar \= FIX → root; odair \= HEAT → fix-complete-root; **oparaj** \= EXPAND/PROJECT → root-**'j'** GLYPH. **THE 'j' EXCEPTION MARKER in the scheduling ring.** The rare 'j' glyph that appeared in herbal Quires F and G (marking special conditions) now appears in the scheduling wheel marking a TEMPORAL EXCEPTION — a time-position requiring non-standard handling.

**R.19 — DOUBLED DAIIN:** sair \= SALT → complete-root; ol \= FLUID; **daiin.daiin** \= **DOUBLE VERIFICATION** ("verified TWICE — absolute confirmation checkpoint"); dal \= FIX → structure; dol \= FIX-FLUID; cheody \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → heat-fix-active; dair \= FIX → complete-root; aly \= structure-active; dairal \= FIX-complete-root-structure; dolar \= FIX-fluid-root; shy \= VIGOROUS-FLOW → active; dor \= FIX → source. **DOUBLED DAIIN — the first double-verification in the scheduling ring.** Where f58r's specification used single daiin at each checkpoint, the scheduling wheel uses DOUBLED daiin at this critical position, indicating a MANDATORY STOP — both parameters must be independently confirmed before proceeding.

**R.21 — TRIPLE-E IN THE SCHEDULING RING:** **todeeey** \= ENERGY → fix-**TRIPLE-E**\-active ("temporal energy at TRIPLE-ESSENCE intensity"); keody ×2 \= body-essence-heat-fix-active (paired); shedy \= TRANSITION-ESSENCE → fixed; shekeepy \= TRANSITION-ESSENCE → body-double-essence-project-active; chdy \= CHANNEL → fixed; sheol \= TRANSITION → fluid; shol \= TRANSITION → fluid; kody \= BODY → heat-fix-active; daly \= FIX → structure-active. **TRIPLE-E IN THE MACRO-CYCLE TRACK.** Certain times of year carry TRIPLE-ESSENCE temporal potency. Compare herbal Quire G's f52r center (master fire seal). This scheduling position is the temporal equivalent of the herbal section's mastery center.

**R.24 — TRIPLE-I (diiirr):** ysheeod \= MOIST-TRANSITION → double-essence-heat-fix; qoteeod \= TRANSMUTE-HEAT → double-essence-heat-fix; qotol \= TRANSMUTE-HEAT → fluid; qoky \= EXTRACT → active; **chckhey** \= CHANNEL → **CKH VALVE** → essence-active ("valve operation in scheduling ring"); shey \= TRANSITION-ESSENCE → active; dcheol \= FIX-VOLATILE → essence-fluid; cheky \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → moist-active; cheo \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → heat; **diiirr** \= FIX → **TRIPLE-I** → double-rotation ("**TRIPLE-I EXTENDED CYCLING** — the same triple-i that encoded extended retort operations in herbal section now encodes an extended TEMPORAL cycle spanning multiple rotations"). **The triple-i says: "This operation takes SO LONG it spans multiple day/night cycles."**

**R.25 — TRIPLE-E \+ 'j' GLYPH \+ DOUBLE DAIIN:** **ydaiin** \= MOIST → fix-double-cycle ("moistened verification"); shody \= TRANSITION → heat-fix-active; **oteeedy** \= TEMPORAL → **TRIPLE-E**\-fixed ("temporal TRIPLE-ESSENCE, FIXED — the maximum temporal intensity, permanently locked"); oteochey \= TEMPORAL → essence-heat-volatile-essence-active; tolchedy \= ENERGY → fluid-volatile-essence-fixed; lsheody \= LAYER-TRANSITION → essence-heat-fix-active; qoky \= EXTRACT → active; **daiin** \= VERIFICATION; **otaj** \= TEMPORAL → **'j'** GLYPH ("temporal SPECIAL CONDITION"). **R.25 contains BOTH triple-e AND 'j' — maximum intensity with an exception marker. Plus two verifications (ydaiin \+ daiin). This is the MOST HEAVILY MARKED ring segment: triple-e \+ 'j' \+ double-verification \= "MAXIMUM INTENSITY, SPECIAL HANDLING, DOUBLY CONFIRMED."**

**R.27 — VALVE-HEAVY SEGMENT:** **daiin** \= VERIFICATION; sheol \= TRANSITION → fluid; **qockhedy** \= EXTRACT → **CKH VALVE**\-essence-fixed ("extraction through valve to fixation"); qokedy \= EXTRACT → essence-fixed; lchey \= LAYER → volatile-essence-active; qokaly \= EXTRACT → structure-active; **shckhy** \= VIGOROUS-FLOW → **CKH VALVE**\-active ("vigorous valve flow"); qotal \= TRANSMUTE-HEAT → structure; otchdy \= TEMPORAL → volatile-heat-fixed. **TWO CKH VALVE references in one segment** (qockhedy \+ shckhy). This temporal position requires DOUBLE VALVE OPERATIONS — two separate flow-control interventions at the same time-position. Compare herbal f51r's 13 CKH tokens (maximum binding). This scheduling segment is the temporal equivalent: maximum flow-control at a critical time.

**W.1 — OUTER BOUNDARY TEXT:** **oiilireo** \= \[non-standard — contains 'i' repetitions and 'n' cluster absent from standard Voynichese\]; **daiin** \= VERIFICATION (standard morpheme embedded in non-standard text); **iriilil** \= \[non-standard\]; **ilnirsireim** \= \[non-standard — contains 'n' glyph\]. This boundary text contains a DAIIN verification embedded within otherwise anomalous text. The standard morpheme confirms the wheel's AUTHORITY — the verification marks it as genuine/authorized. The surrounding non-standard characters may encode a title, a proper name, a numbering system, or a phrase transliterated from another script (Latin? Arabic? Hebrew?).

---

### **PLAIN-ENGLISH PROCESS DESCRIPTION**

F66r is a **MULTI-TRACK SCHEDULING SPREADSHEET** rendered as a circular diagram. It is the production scheduling dashboard for the entire pharmaceutical year.

**Reading the wheel:**

1. **Find your current date's ANGULAR POSITION** on the outermost ring  
2. **Read the ELEMENT MARKER** (M-series single character) — which element dominates NOW?  
3. **Read the COLUMN HEADER** (L-series label) — what operation is AVAILABLE now?  
4. **Read the RING TEXT** (R-series) — what is the DETAILED PROCEDURE for this time position?  
5. **Check for EXCEPTION MARKERS** ('j' glyphs, double-daiin, triple-e) — any special conditions?

**Three operational bands** (marked by \= terminators):

* **R.1–R.7** (7 segments): FOUNDATION BAND — initial setup and first verification  
* **R.8–R.13** (6 segments): PROCESS BAND — active operations with second verification  
* **R.14–R.32** (19 segments): EXECUTION BAND — detailed procedures including triple-e peaks, 'j' exceptions, valve operations, and triple-i extended cycles

**The wheel encodes:**

* 15 operational categories (complete alchemical repertoire)  
* 34 elemental governance positions (which element dominates when)  
* 32 detailed procedural descriptions (what to do at each position)  
* 7+ verification checkpoints (daiin markers in ring texts)  
* 2+ valve operations (CKH references in ring texts)  
* 2 triple-e peaks (maximum temporal intensity positions)  
* 1 triple-i extended cycle (multi-day operation marker)  
* 1 'j' exception (special temporal condition)

This is functionally identical to a modern production scheduling system — a Gantt chart rendered in circular medieval format. The practitioner consults this chart daily to determine what operations the current temporal position supports.

### **CROSS-EXAMINATION WITH ALCHEMICAL & MEDICAL STANDARDS**

**Comparison with Volvelle Instruments:** Medieval astronomical manuscripts frequently included rotating paper disks (volvelles) that allowed practitioners to calculate temporal positions. Peter Apian's *Astronomicum Caesareum* (1540) contains elaborate volvelles with concentric rings carrying different data tracks — exactly the format of f66r. The Voynich wheel is a STATIC version of a volvelle: instead of rotating disks, it encodes all positions on a single fixed diagram.

**Comparison with Sacrobosco's *Tractatus de Sphaera*:** Sacrobosco's influential 13th-century astronomy textbook uses concentric-ring diagrams to illustrate the celestial spheres. F66r's concentric rings follow the same visual convention but apply it to SCHEDULING rather than cosmology — the rings encode operational data, not planetary orbits.

**The Alchemical Operations in 15 Labels:** The 15 L-series labels map the complete *opus magnum* onto the annual calendar. Compare with George Ripley's *Twelve Gates of Alchemy* (1471) which also structures the alchemical *opus* as a temporal sequence: Calcination → Dissolution → Separation → Conjunction → Putrefaction → Congelation → Cibation → Sublimation → Fermentation → Exaltation → Multiplication → Projection. Ripley's 12 gates map to a 12-sign zodiac; f66r's 15 labels provide FINER temporal resolution than Ripley's system.

**The Elemental Grid:** The M-series markers distribute the four elements (plus additional operational modes) around the wheel. This matches the elemental quality theory taught in medieval universities: each time-period has a DOMINANT element that constrains which operations are possible. The predominance of Earth (d=4) and Quintessence (y=4) markers confirms the pharmaceutical bias — most operations involve fixation (Earth) and extraction (Quintessence).

**The Triple-E and Triple-I in Temporal Context:** The appearance of both triple-e (maximum essence) and triple-i (extended cycling) in the scheduling ring confirms that these VML concentration markers are DOMAIN-INDEPENDENT: they operate identically in pharmaceutical products (herbal section) and temporal scheduling (astronomical section). This universality is the strongest evidence for VML as a genuine systematic grammar rather than a random or decorative notation.

# **FOLIO F66V — PAGE 115**

## **EXECUTION RULES — THE TRANSITION ENGINE**

| Property | Value |

| **Illustration** | **TEXT-ONLY** — 13 paragraphs of dense operational text. No diagram. |
| **Paragraphs** | 13 (P.1–P.13) |
| **Risk Level** | REFERENCE |
| **Distinction** | **HEAVIEST PHASE-SHIFT (ok-) MORPHOLOGY in the entire manuscript. The TRANSITION ENGINE — specifies how to move between temporal states.** |

---

### **PHYSICAL DESCRIPTION & IMAGE ANALYSIS**

Text-only verso of f66r. Where the recto carried the magnificent circular scheduling diagram, the verso carries 13 paragraphs of operational text that specify the EXECUTION RULES for the scheduling wheel. This is a deliberate pairing: the recto shows WHEN (the visual calendar); the verso specifies HOW (the operational instructions).

Thirteen paragraphs of varying length arranged in standard text format. The paragraphs fall into three structural blocks, each terminated by a distinct closing pattern. The text is densely packed with phase-shift (ok-) morphemes — more ok- tokens per line than any other page in the manuscript.

No illustration is present, matching f58r's text-only format. The astronomical section's text-only pages (f58r, f65v, f66v) form a trio of SPECIFICATION DOCUMENTS that frame the illustrated diagrams: f58r defines the SYSTEM, f65v provides QA REFERENCE, and f66v specifies EXECUTION. The diagrams (f66r, f67r1–f67v2, f68r1–f69r, f70r2–f73v) are the ILLUSTRATED MACHINES that these text-only pages instruct the practitioner to operate.

**Physical note on recto/verso pairing:** F66r (diagram) and f66v (text) form a BIFOLIO PAIR — the diagram faces outward when the book lies open, and the execution rules face inward. The practitioner SEES the wheel first, then TURNS THE PAGE to read the execution instructions. This is a deliberate pedagogical sequence: VISUALIZE the schedule → READ the execution rules → OPERATE.

FEELS LIKE the back page of an instrument panel manual — the front page (f66r) shows the dashboard layout with all its dials and indicators; the back page (f66v) lists the OPERATING PROCEDURES: "When indicator A reads X, perform procedure Y. When transitioning from State 1 to State 2, follow sequence Z." The transition engine that makes the scheduling wheel ACTUALLY WORK.

---

### **ASTRONOMICAL IDENTIFICATION**

| Field | Data |
| ----- | ----- |
| **Subject** | Execution rules for f66r scheduling wheel — operational text |
| **Astronomical Content** | Phase-transition specifications for moving between temporal states encoded in the scheduling calendar |
| **Classical Framework** | Matches *regulae* (rules) sections in medieval computational astronomy texts — instructions for operating tables and instruments |
| **Historical Parallel** | Comparable to the *canones* (operational instructions) that accompany astronomical tables in the Alfonsine Tables tradition and in the *Zij* (astronomical handbook) tradition of Islamic astronomy |

**Formula-Astronomical Alignment:** The ok- (phase-shift) dominance is the KEY FINDING. The scheduling wheel (f66r) defines POSITIONS; this page defines TRANSITIONS between positions. In any control system, the transitions are more complex than the positions — moving from State A to State B requires specific procedures that depend on BOTH the starting state AND the ending state. F66v encodes these transition functions. The ok- prefix means "phase-shift" — the operational character of CHANGING FROM ONE PHASE TO ANOTHER. This page is dominated by the CHANGE OPERATION because it specifies nothing BUT changes.

FEELS LIKE the state-transition table for a finite-state machine — given your current state and the target state, THIS is the procedure to execute the transition. The scheduling wheel tells you WHERE you are and WHERE you need to be; f66v tells you HOW TO GET THERE.

### **Phase-Shift Dominance Analysis**

The ok- morphemes in f66v include: okeodof, okshedy, okeedy, okchdy, okchdal, okedy, okechdy, okaiin, okchdy, okeshy, okchdy, okees, okedy, okchdy. Nearly every paragraph contains at LEAST one ok- token. Compare:

* **F58r** (specification): OTAL- dominant (temporal-structure) — defines WHAT the system IS  
* **F66r** (schedule): Mixed vocabulary — describes WHAT IS HAPPENING at each position  
* **F66v** (execution): OK- dominant (phase-shift) — describes HOW TO CHANGE between positions

The three pages form a COMPLETE CONTROL SYSTEM: DEFINE (f58r) → DISPLAY (f66r) → EXECUTE (f66v).

### **VML TOKEN-BY-TOKEN TRANSLATION**

**P.1 — OPENING: THE PHASE-SHIFT DECLARATION:** **okeodof** \= PHASE-SHIFT → essence-heat-fix-**FORMATIVE** ("phase-shifting essence through heat-fixation TO THE GROWTH STATE — the transition BEGINS with a phase-shift to Venus's formative principle"); sheod \= TRANSITION-ESSENCE → heat-fix ("transitional essence heat-fixed"); ychoopy \= MOIST-VOLATILE → heat-heat-project-active ("moistened volatile, doubly-heated, projected"); opch \= EXPAND/PROJECT → volatile ("projected volatile"); dal \= FIX → structure; dorshefy \= FIX → source-transition-essence-formative-active ("fixation at source through transitional formative essence"); ytody \= MOIST-ENERGY → temporal-heat-fix-active ("moistened temporal energy heat-fixed"); da\*deam \= FIX → \[damaged\]-fix-essence-union

**P.1 ANALYSIS:** The page OPENS with **okeodof** — a phase-shift to the FORMATIVE state. The first instruction in the execution rules is: "Phase-shift to GROWTH." Before any other transition can occur, the system must be in its GENERATIVE state. This matches the alchemical principle that all operations begin from the *prima materia* — the unformed, generative potential. Venus's growth principle (the f-atom in \-of) is the STARTING CONDITION for all subsequent transitions.

**P.2 — HEAVY PHASE-SHIFT PROCESSING:** teodal \= ENERGY-TEMPORAL → essence-heat-fix-structure; tchdy \= ENERGY-VOLATILE → fixed; dshey \= FIX-TRANSITION → essence-active; **okshedy** \= PHASE-SHIFT → transition-essence-fixed ("phase-shifted transitional essence, fixed"); **okeedy** \= PHASE-SHIFT → double-essence-fixed ("phase-shifted double-essence, fixed"); dcheeky \= FIX-VOLATILE → double-essence-active; daldy \= FIX → structure-fixed; qotal \= TRANSMUTE-HEAT → structure; sy \= SALT → active

**P.2 ANALYSIS:** Two consecutive ok- phase-shifts (okshedy, okeedy) process transitional essence and double-essence respectively. The transitions are SEQUENCED: first shift the simple transitional form, then shift the intensified double-essence form. Each shift ends in fixation (-dy/-edy). This is a STEP-WISE TRANSITION: don't try to shift everything at once — shift the simple fraction first, verify it's fixed, then shift the concentrated fraction.

**P.3 — TEMPORAL STRUCTURE ACTIVE:** ytos \= MOIST-ENERGY → heat-salt; s \= salt; ar \= root; sheeky \= TRANSITION-ESSENCE → double-essence-active; **okechdy** \= PHASE-SHIFT → essence-volatile-heat-fixed ("phase-shifted volatile essence, heat-fixed"); **okchdal** \= PHASE-SHIFT → volatile-heat-fix-structure ("phase-shifted volatile, structurally fixed"); dar \= FIX → root; **otal** \= TEMPORAL → structure ("temporal structure — scheduling architecture"); chody \= VOLATILE-HEAT → heat-fix-active; cheky \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → moist-active

**P.3 ANALYSIS:** **Otal** appears — the temporal-structure morpheme that dominated f58r's specification. The execution rules REFERENCE the specification architecture: "Within the temporal structure (otal), perform phase-shifts (okechdy, okchdal) to fix volatile essence into structural form (dar)." The execution rules operate WITHIN the framework the specification defined.

**P.4 — FIRST VERIFICATION \+ FIRST VALVE:** shokeshy \= TRANSITION-HEAT → essence-transition-active; **daiin** \= **FIRST VERIFICATION** — execution block 1 verified; cheos \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → heat-salt; chty \= CHANNEL-CONDUIT → active; dol \= FIX-FLUID; **chckhy** \= CHANNEL → **CKH VALVE** → active ("**FIRST VALVE** — flow control engaged at verification point"); dal \= FIX → structure; ko \= BODY → heat; dal \= FIX → structure; chekal \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → body-structure; dal \= FIX → structure

**P.4 ANALYSIS:** The FIRST DAIIN and FIRST CKH VALVE appear together. The pattern: VERIFY → ENGAGE VALVE. After confirming the phase-shift sequence is correct (daiin), immediately engage flow control (chckhy) to regulate the transition. Compare herbal patterns where daiin and CKH often co-occurred (f51r's valve-heavy verification page). The valve appears AT THE VERIFICATION POINT because this is where the system transitions from one state to the next — flow control is critical during state changes.

**P.5 — VENUS UNION \+ FIRST TERMINATOR:** shdy \= VIGOROUS-FLOW → fixed; shed \= TRANSITION-ESSENCE → fix; **fam** \= **FORMATIVE → UNION** ("**VENUS GROWTH PRINCIPLE UNITED** — the f-atom achieves union, meaning Venus's growth force has been successfully combined into the product"); qokedy \= EXTRACT → essence-fixed; chokal \= VOLATILE-HEAT → essence-structure; dal \= FIX → structure **\= FIRST PARAGRAPH TERMINATOR**

**P.5 ANALYSIS:** **fam** (formative-union) is EXCEPTIONALLY RARE — the f-atom (Venus's growth principle) combined with \-am (union). This means: "The growth force has been JOINED into the product." In astrological terms, Venus has completed her work — the growth phase has been successfully incorporated. The \= terminator seals Block 1 (P.1–P.5): from initial phase-shift (okeodof) through Venus union (fam), verified (daiin) and valve-controlled (chckhy). **BLOCK 1: GROWTH → VERIFICATION → FLOW CONTROL → VENUS UNION → SEALED.**

**P.6 — BLOCK 2 OPENING: VALVE-SHEATHED TRANSITION:** tchod \= ENERGY-VOLATILE → heat-fix; sheody \= TRANSITION-ESSENCE → heat-fix-active; **shckhed** \= VIGOROUS-FLOW → **CKH VALVE** → essence-fix ("vigorous flow through valve, essence-fixed — **THE VALVE SHEATHES THE TRANSITION**"); chos \= VOLATILE-HEAT → heat-salt; chor \= VOLATILE-HEAT → source; sheo \= TRANSITION-ESSENCE → heat; keody \= BODY → essence-heat-fix-active; chpar \= CHANNEL-PROJECT → root; **sheopam** \= TRANSITION-ESSENCE → heat-project-union ("transitional essence projected to union")

**P.6 ANALYSIS:** Block 2 opens with shckhed — the valve WRAPPING AROUND the transition. Where Block 1 engaged the valve AT the verification point, Block 2 uses the valve CONTINUOUSLY during the transition. The flow-control has shifted from checkpoint-based (Block 1\) to continuous (Block 2). This progressive valve engagement mirrors herbal evolution where valve operations became increasingly integrated from Quire F to Quire G.

**P.7 — SECOND VALVE \+ EXTRACT:** qokeos \= EXTRACT → essence-heat-salt; sheody \= TRANSITION → heat-fix-active; cheke\*r \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → body-essence-\[damaged\]-root; chody \= VOLATILE-HEAT → heat-fix-active; ko \= BODY → heat; tody \= ENERGY → heat-fix-active; qotchdy \= TRANSMUTE-HEAT → volatile-heat-fixed; **chckhy** \= **SECOND VALVE**; tchdy \= ENERGY-VOLATILE → fixed

**P.8 — VALVE COMPOUND \+ SECOND TERMINATOR:** **dchckheedy** \= FIX → **CKH VALVE** → double-essence-fixed ("fixation THROUGH the valve at DOUBLE-ESSENCE intensity — **THE MOST COMPLEX VALVE TOKEN in the manuscript**"); cheody \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → heat-fix-active; qokchdy \= EXTRACT → volatile-heat-fixed; qokol \= EXTRACT → fluid; keedy \= BODY → double-essence-fixed; cheky \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → moist-active; chety \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → temporal-active; kody \= BODY → heat-fix-active **\= SECOND TERMINATOR**

**P.8 ANALYSIS:** **dchckheedy** is the MOST COMPLEX VALVE TOKEN in the manuscript — d+ckh+ee+dy \= fix \+ valve \+ double-essence \+ fixed. Fixation THROUGH the valve at DOUBLE-ESSENCE intensity. This is a COMPOUND OPERATION: the valve isn't just controlling flow — it's being used as part of the FIXATION PROCESS ITSELF. The material passes through the valve and is FIXED during passage. **BLOCK 2: CONTINUOUS VALVE → EXTRACTION → VALVE-FIXATION AT DOUBLE-ESSENCE → SEALED.**

**P.9 — BLOCK 3 OPENING:** pody \= PROJECT-FLUID → heat-fix-active; sheody \= TRANSITION → heat-fix-active; chpa \= CHANNEL-PROJECT; dar \= FIX → root; sheey \= TRANSITION-ESSENCE → active; **feedly** \= **FORMATIVE-ESSENCE**\-double-essence-layer-active ("Venus growth essence at DOUBLE-ESSENCE in LAYERED form — **SECOND F-ATOM**"); cheos \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → heat-salt; **eesey** \= TRIPLE-ESSENCE-salt-active ("**TRIPLE-E SALT** — maximum essence crystallized"); kchy \= BODY → volatile-active; aopchal \= \[a\]-EXPAND/PROJECT → volatile-structure

**P.9 ANALYSIS:** Block 3 opens with TWO significant tokens: **feedly** (Venus growth at double-essence, layered) and **eesey** (triple-E salt). The f-atom returns at INTENSIFIED LEVEL (double-essence), and the triple-e appears as CRYSTALLIZED SALT. This is the CULMINATION: Venus's growth reaches double-essence and crystallizes at triple-essence intensity. Compare herbal Quire G's f52r (master fire seal \+ 9 unions) — Block 3 of the execution rules achieves the same culmination in temporal form.

**P.10 — TRIPLE VERIFICATION:** dshal \= FIX-TRANSITION → structure; keedy \= BODY → double-essence-fixed; qokyr \= EXTRACT → moist-rotation; **okaiin** \= PHASE-SHIFT → double-cycle ("**PHASE-SHIFT VERIFIED**"); dol \= FIX-FLUID; kal \= BODY → structure; **daiin** \= **SECOND DAIIN — DOUBLE VERIFICATION** (okaiin \+ daiin \= phase-shift verified AND fixation verified); **otal** \= TEMPORAL → structure; dakar \= FIX → essence-body-root; **otam** \= TEMPORAL → union ("temporal union — the scheduling system's conjunction")

**P.10 ANALYSIS:** Two verification tokens (okaiin \+ daiin) create a DOUBLE VERIFICATION — the phase-shift is verified AND the fixation is verified. Plus otal (temporal structure) and otam (temporal union) confirm the scheduling architecture is correctly conjoined. This is the QUALITY GATE for Block 3: everything verified before the final closure.

**P.11 — SALT COMPLETION \+ VENUS GROWTH \+ TEMPORAL COMPLETION:** yteeod \= MOIST-ENERGY → double-essence-heat-fix; **aiin** \= DOUBLE-CYCLE; shekeod \= TRANSITION-ESSENCE → body-essence-heat-fix; **saiin** \= SALT → double-cycle ("**SALT CRYSTALLIZATION VERIFIED**"); **ykofar** \= MOIST-BODY → **FORMATIVE**\-root ("**VENUS GROWTH at ROOT** — the f-atom GROUNDED, growth principle ROOTED"); **otaiin** \= TEMPORAL → double-cycle ("**TEMPORAL SCHEDULE VERIFIED**"); otar \= TEMPORAL → root; chedy \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → fixed; kara \= BODY → root

**P.11 ANALYSIS:** Three verification tokens in one line (aiin \+ saiin \+ otaiin). TRIPLE VERIFICATION: cycle confirmed, salt crystallization confirmed, temporal schedule confirmed. Plus **ykofar** \= Venus's growth principle GROUNDED at root. The growth that began in P.1 (okeodof — phase-shift to formative) now ends ROOTED (ykofar). The growth cycle is complete: from aerial initiation to rooted grounding.

**P.12 — THIRD VALVE \+ DOUBLE BODY:** qekar \= \[uncertain\]; okedy \= PHASE-SHIFT → essence-fixed; cheky \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → moist-active; dal \= FIX → structure; chekal \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → body-structure; **chckhy** \= **THIRD VALVE** ("valve engaged for THIRD TIME — one valve per block"); **kal.kal** \= BODY → structure × 2 ("**DOUBLED BODY-STRUCTURE** — reinforced material framework"); dar \= FIX → root; chkchody \= CHANNEL-BODY → volatile-heat-fix-active

**P.12 ANALYSIS:** The THIRD chckhy valve — one per operational block. Block 1 had the valve at the verification point (P.4). Block 2 had it continuous (P.6–P.8). Block 3 has it at P.12: late in the block, near the closure. The valve's POSITION within each block shifts: checkpoint → continuous → closing. Progressive integration. Plus **kal.kal** (doubled body-structure) \= REINFORCED framework, matching the intensification pattern across blocks.

**P.13 — FINAL CLOSURE:** ydees \= MOIST → fix-double-essence-salt; shey \= TRANSITION-ESSENCE → active; **daiin** \= **THIRD AND FINAL DAIIN** ("final verification"); dal \= FIX → structure; kal \= BODY → structure; **ykedaiin** \= MOIST-BODY → essence-fix-double-cycle ("moistened body essence fixation VERIFIED — compound verification"); shedar \= TRANSITION-ESSENCE → fix-root; **okchdy** \= PHASE-SHIFT → volatile-heat-fixed ("FINAL PHASE-SHIFT — volatile heat FIXED permanently"); **oty=** \= TEMPORAL → active **\= FINAL PARAGRAPH TERMINATOR**

**P.13 ANALYSIS:** The page ends with **oty=** — temporal-active, terminated. The execution rules close by declaring the temporal system ACTIVE and SEALED. Compare herbal f57r's cphedam (COMBINE) — the herbal section ended with combination; the execution rules end with temporal ACTIVATION. The factory's products were combined; the factory's clock is now running.

**THREE OPERATIONAL BLOCKS** (marked by \= terminators at P.5, P.8, P.13):

**BLOCK 1 (P.1–P.5): GROWTH INITIATION**

* Opens with phase-shift to Venus growth (okeodof)  
* Steps through increasing phase-shift complexity (okshedy → okeedy → okechdy → okchdal)

* Closes with Venus UNION achieved (fam, P.5) — growth incorporated into product  
* SEALED

**BLOCK 2 (P.6–P.8): CONTINUOUS VALVE-CONTROLLED EXTRACTION**

* Most complex valve token in manuscript (dchckheedy — fix through valve at double-essence)  
* SEALED

* Venus growth ROOTED (ykofar — growth principle grounded)  
* Third valve (chckhy, P.12) \+ doubled body-structure (kal.kal)  
* Final phase-shift locked (okchdy) \+ temporal system ACTIVE (oty=)  
* SEALED

**PROGRESSIVE INTENSIFICATION ACROSS BLOCKS:**
