### **CROSS-EXAMINATION WITH ALCHEMICAL & MEDICAL STANDARDS**

**Comparison with *Canones* Tradition:** Medieval astronomical tables were always accompanied by *canones* — operational instructions explaining how to use the tables. The Alfonsine Tables (compiled c. 1252 for Alfonso X of Castile) include extensive *canones* explaining how to enter the tables, how to interpolate between listed values, and how to transition between different sections. F66v serves the identical function for the f66r scheduling wheel: it is the *canones* that explain how to OPERATE the calendar.

**The Venus Growth Arc (okeodof → fam → feedly → ykofar):** Venus's growth principle undergoes a complete arc across the three blocks: INITIATED (phase-shift to formative) → UNITED (formative union) → INTENSIFIED (double-essence layered) → GROUNDED (rooted at body). This four-stage Venus arc matches the classical doctrine of Venus's influence in temporal pharmacy: Venus rules the VEGETATIVE stage of any process — the period of growth and development between the initial stimulus and the final fixation. The execution rules encode Venus's complete influence cycle within 13 paragraphs.

**The Progressive Valve Integration:** The valve shifts from checkpoint (Block 1\) to continuous (Block 2\) to closing (Block 3). In medieval distillation practice, the stopcock (valve) was used in three modes: (1) opened briefly for sampling (checkpoint), (2) partially opened for continuous controlled flow (continuous), and (3) sealed for final containment (closing). The three-block valve progression in f66v exactly mirrors these three modes of real distillation valve operation.

**The Triple Verification in Block 3:** Five verification tokens in two paragraphs (P.10–P.11) is the densest verification concentration outside f58r's specification. In pharmaceutical quality assurance, the FINAL verification before product release is always the most rigorous — multiple independent checks must agree before the product leaves the laboratory. Block 3's quintu-verification serves this function: the culmination phase requires the MOST checks because errors here waste the entire preceding effort.

**Comparison with Geber's *Summa Perfectionis*:** Geber (pseudo-Jabir, 13th c.) describes pharmaceutical operations in three stages: *preparatio* (preparation/growth), *alteratio* (alteration/processing), and *fixio* (fixation/completion). F66v's three blocks follow this sequence precisely: Block 1 \= preparatio (Venus growth initiated), Block 2 \= alteratio (valve-controlled extraction), Block 3 \= fixio (culmination, rooting, activation).

# **FOLIO F67R1 — PAGE 116**

## **LUNAR MONTH-WHEEL — THE MONTHLY CLOCK**

| Property | Value |

| **Folio** | f67r1 (recto, sub-page 1\) |

| **Function** | LUNAR CALENDAR — 12-sector moon-phase calendar determining monthly operation types (Resolution Level 3 of 6\) |
| **Illustration** | CIRCULAR DIAGRAM with 12 wedge sectors radiating from central point, moon faces at sector boundaries, 3 concentric text rings, 12 star/nymph labels |
| **Text Segments** | P (4 paragraphs), R1 (outer ring), R2 (middle ring), R3 (inner ring), S (12 sector labels) |
| **Risk Level** | REFERENCE |

---

### **PHYSICAL DESCRIPTION & IMAGE ANALYSIS**

A circular diagram divided into **12 WEDGE SECTORS** radiating from a central point. Each sector represents one LUNAR MONTH — one complete cycle from new moon through full moon and back to new. The 12 sectors create a complete ANNUAL WHEEL showing all 12 monthly cycles.

**MOON FACES** appear at sector boundaries: alternating light (waxing/full) and dark (waning/new) lunar symbols mark the PHASE TRANSITIONS between months. The practitioner identifies the current lunar phase by finding the appropriate boundary marker, then reads inward to determine which operations are available.

**12 STAR/NYMPH LABELS (S-series):** Positioned within the sectors, each encoding the operational character of that month. These are SHORT labels (1–2 tokens each) — compressed scheduling codes that tell the practitioner at a glance what kind of work this month supports.

**3 CONCENTRIC TEXT RINGS** wrap the diagram:

* **R1 (outer ring):** \~35 tokens — the longest ring text. Contains the monthly MACRO-RULES for the entire year. Includes a chockhy (CKH valve) reference, triple-e tokens (sheeer), and a remarkable closing sequence: **dardarar** (fix-root × 3 \= TRIPLE ROOTING) followed by **otar.dar.okarar=** (temporal-root, fix-root, phase-root-root \= ROOT EVERYTHING).  
* **R2 (middle ring):** \~35 tokens — the monthly PARAMETERS. Contains daiin verification, saiin salt completion, the rare 'j' glyph (chetjy), and double-e tokens.  
* **R3 (inner/kernel ring):** \~30 tokens — the monthly CORE CLOCK. Contains triple-e (oteeey), multiple oteodal temporal-fixation commands, and closes with **chparaj** (channel-project-root-'j' \= another 'j' exception).

**4 PARAGRAPHS (P.1–P.4):** Below or beside the diagram, providing the operational preamble — parameters that apply to ALL months before any specific month is consulted.

**Physical construction notes:** The 12-sector division matches the 12 zodiac signs, confirming this wheel SYNCHRONIZES with the zodiac pages (f70r2–f73v). The 12 sectors \= 12 months \= 12 zodiac signs \= a single unified annual calendar. The pencil letters 'a', 'b', 'c' noted by Zandbergen at the top corners of f67r2 (adjacent sub-page) suggest later cataloguing of the fold-out sub-pages.

FEELS LIKE the MONTH DIAL on a grandfather clock — the outer mechanism you consult to determine "what month is it?" before consulting the inner mechanisms (hour, minute, second). The lunar month-wheel answers the MONTHLY question: "Given the current lunar phase, what class of pharmaceutical operations should I be performing?" The answer depends on where the moon sits in its cycle: dissolution when waxing, maturation at full, purification when waning, fixation at dark.

---

### **ASTRONOMICAL IDENTIFICATION**

| Field | Data |
| ----- | ----- |
| **Subject** | Lunar month calendar — monthly resolution scheduling |
| **Astronomical Content** | 12-sector lunar cycle mapping pharmaceutical operations to lunar phases |
| **Classical Framework** | Medieval lunar pharmacy (*medicina lunaris*) — all liquid-phase operations governed by lunar light |
| **Historical Parallel** | Comparable to lunar medical calendars in *Très Riches Heures du Duc de Berry*, Petrus de Dacia's *computus*, and the *Calendarium* of Regiomontanus. Also matches Islamic *qamariyyāt* (lunar medicine) traditions transmitted through Salerno |

**Formula-Astronomical Alignment:** The lunar governance of pharmaceutical operations was UNIVERSAL in medieval practice. The *Circa Instans* explicitly states that gathering simples, compounding, and administering medicines should follow lunar phases. The Salernitan *Regimen Sanitatis* prescribes bloodletting by lunar phase. The *Secretum Secretorum* (pseudo-Aristotelian, widely circulated) links every bodily process to the moon. F67r1 encodes this universal system in VML — the 12 sectors divide the lunar year into 12 operational zones, each with its own character.

**The Lunar Operational Quadrants:**

* **New Moon → First Quarter:** DISSOLUTION — increasing lunar light \= increasing fluid activity. Ideal for extractions, dissolutions, infusions.  
* **First Quarter → Full Moon:** MATURATION — growing lunar influence. Ideal for fermentation, digestion, ripening.  
* **Full Moon → Third Quarter:** PURIFICATION — declining lunar light \= decreasing impurities. Ideal for filtration, separation, decanting.  
* **Third Quarter → New Moon:** FIXATION — dying lunar light \= solidification. Ideal for crystallization, coagulation, precipitation.

FEELS LIKE the production calendar on a brewery wall — "January: malt preparation. February: mashing. March: fermentation. April: conditioning. May: first draw." Each month has its designated operation, determined by the season and the moon.

### **VML TOKEN-BY-TOKEN TRANSLATION — SECTOR LABELS (The 12 Months)**

| Month | Label | VML | Lunar Operation |
| ----- | ----- | ----- | ----- |
| **S.1** | otaldy | TEMPORAL → structure-fixed | **"Schedule LOCKED"** — initialization month. The annual cycle's first month is structurally fixed: SET the framework. |
| **S.2** | otoky | TEMPORAL → heat-body-active | **"Schedule HEATED and embodied"** — the timing system activates in material. |
| **S.3** | seeyar | SALT-ESSENCE → essence-active-root | **"Double-essence salt ROOTED"** — crystallization rooted at base. |
| **S.4** | ykas.asy | MOIST-BODY → essence-salt \+ essence-salt-active | **"Moistened body salted TWICE"** — double salt formation (compare f65v's \*sas). |
| **S.5** | sosainr | SALT → heat-salt-complete-rotation | **"Salt fully rotated"** — crystallization cycle complete. |
| **S.6** | oteey.dar | TEMPORAL → double-essence-active \+ FIX-ROOT | **"Timed double-essence FIXED at root"** — scheduled intensification grounded. |
| **S.7** | ytodaiir | MOIST-ENERGY → temporal-heat-fix-doubly-complete | **"Moistened temporal fixation DOUBLY VERIFIED"** — double completion check. |
| **S.8** | **sheoraj** | TRANSITION-ESSENCE → heat-rotation-**'j'** | **"Transitional essence rotated — SPECIAL CONDITION"** — the 'j' exception marks this month as non-standard. |
| **S.9** | ykeeody | MOIST-BODY → double-essence-heat-fix-active | **"Moistened body double-essence heat-fixed"** — product formation month. |
| **S.10** | okeol.sal | PHASE-SHIFT → essence-fluid \+ SALT | **"Phase-shifted essence-fluid SALTED"** — crystallization from phase-shifted fluid. |
| **S.11** | okeey.sar | PHASE-SHIFT → double-essence-active \+ SALT-ROOT | **"Phase-shifted double-essence SALT-ROOTED"** — intensified salt grounded. |
| **S.12** | dalary | FIX → structure-root-active | **"FIXED, ROOTED, ACTIVE"** — annual closure. Everything fixed and rooted. |

**THE 'j' GLYPH AT S.8:** Month 8 (counting from the annual start) carries the 'j' exception marker. This is the ONLY month with a non-standard condition. In a 12-month cycle, month 8 from the spring equinox \= approximately NOVEMBER (Scorpio) — the deepest transformation month, when Mars-ruled Water/Fixed governs. The exception marker at this position is consistent with Scorpio's character as the month requiring the most non-standard handling.

**THE ANNUAL ARC IN 12 LABELS:**

* Months 1–2 (S.1–S.2): INITIALIZATION — schedule locked, then activated  
* Months 3–5 (S.3–S.5): SALT FORMATION — double salt, full rotation  
* Months 6–7 (S.6–S.7): INTENSIFICATION — double-essence fixed, doubly verified  
* Month 8 (S.8): EXCEPTION — 'j' marks non-standard operations  
* Months 9–11 (S.9–S.11): PRODUCT FORMATION — double-essence products, phase-shifted salts  
* Month 12 (S.12): CLOSURE — everything fixed, rooted, active

---

### **VML TOKEN-BY-TOKEN TRANSLATION — KEY RING TEXT HIGHLIGHTS**

**R1 — OUTER RING CLOSING SEQUENCE:** The outer ring ends with a remarkable ROOT-FIXATION cascade:

* **dar** \= fix-root  
* **darchdy** \= fix-root-volatile-heat-fixed  
* **dardarar** \= fix-root-fix-root-root \= **TRIPLE ROOTING** — the most emphatic fixation in the manuscript  
* **otar** \= temporal-root — the schedule ROOTED  
* **dar** \= fix-root (again)  
* **okarar=** \= phase-root-root \= phase-shift DOUBLY ROOTED, TERMINATED

**SEVEN dar- (fix-root) tokens in the final 8 words.** The outer ring of the lunar wheel HAMMERS fixation into place. Every last instruction is ROOT, ROOT, ROOT. The lunar calendar's macro-rule: at the end of every cycle, FIX EVERYTHING AT ROOT. This is the pharmaceutical year's closing instruction: don't leave anything unfixed, ungrounded, or volatile.

**R1 — VALVE REFERENCE:** chockhy \= VOLATILE-HEAT → CKH VALVE → active. The CKH valve appears in the lunar calendar's outer ring — flow control is part of the MACRO-CYCLE rules, not just individual operations. The valve governs year-level operations, not just single procedures.

**R2 — MIDDLE RING 'j' GLYPH:** **chetjy** \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → energy-**'j'**\-active. The 'j' glyph appears in the middle ring alongside chedaiin (verified volatile essence). The 'j' in the middle ring and the 'j' in sector label S.8 create TWO 'j' references in the lunar wheel — one in the monthly schedule and one in the parametric ring. The exception is DOUBLY ENCODED.

**R3 — INNER/KERNEL RING:** Contains **oteeey** \= TEMPORAL → **TRIPLE-E**\-active — temporal triple-essence in the KERNEL of the lunar wheel. The innermost timing atom carries maximum intensity. Also contains **dararal** \= fix-root-root-structure \= triple-fix at the structural level. And closes with **chparaj** \= channel-project-root-**'j'** — the THIRD 'j' glyph on this page. **Three 'j' glyphs total:** S.8 (sector), R2 (middle ring), R3 (kernel). The exception condition permeates ALL THREE LEVELS of the lunar calendar.

**P.3 — 'j' IN PARAGRAPHS:** ycheos \= MOIST-VOLATILE → essence-salt; o.**j** \= heat \+ **'j' GLYPH** (FOURTH 'j' on this page\!); **eeeor** \= **TRIPLE-E** → source ("triple-essence projecting outward"); aiin \= DOUBLE-CYCLE; okesoe \= PHASE-SHIFT → salt-heat-essence; ar \= root; **aj** \= root-**'j'** (FIFTH 'j'\!); shchy \= VIGOROUS-FLOW → volatile-active; dy\*aiin \= FIX → \[damaged\]-VERIFIED; **daj** \= FIX → **'j'** (SIXTH 'j'\!).

**SIX 'j' GLYPHS ON F67R1.** This is the HIGHEST 'j' CONCENTRATION in the entire manuscript. The lunar month-wheel is SATURATED with exception markers. Why? Because the MOON is the most variable, most unpredictable celestial body — its cycle is approximately but not exactly regular (29.53 days, not 30), it doesn't precisely align with the solar year (12 lunar months ≈ 354 days, not 365), and lunar eclipses create additional exceptions. The 'j' saturation encodes the INHERENT IRREGULARITY of lunar timekeeping.

---

### **PLAIN-ENGLISH PROCESS DESCRIPTION**

F67r1 is the **LUNAR MONTH-WHEEL** — the monthly resolution layer (Level 3\) of the manuscript's six-level temporal hierarchy.

**Reading the wheel:**

1. Determine the CURRENT LUNAR PHASE (new, waxing, full, waning)  
2. Find the corresponding SECTOR (1–12) by matching the moon-face boundary markers  
3. Read the SECTOR LABEL to determine this month's operational character  
4. Consult the RING TEXTS for detailed parameters

**Key discoveries:**

* **12 sector labels** trace an annual arc: initialization → salt formation → intensification → exception → product formation → closure

* Waxing moon \= DISSOLUTION operations (increasing fluid activity)  
* Full moon \= MATURATION operations (peak lunar influence)  
* Waning moon \= PURIFICATION operations (declining impurities)  
* Dark moon \= FIXATION operations (solidification/crystallization)

### **CROSS-EXAMINATION WITH ALCHEMICAL & MEDICAL STANDARDS**

**Lunar Medicine (*Medicina Lunaris*):** The governance of medical and pharmaceutical operations by lunar phases was codified in multiple medieval texts. The *Secretum Secretorum* (pseudo-Aristotle, widely circulated from 12th c.) prescribes: "Gather herbs when the moon waxes; distill when the moon is full; separate when the moon wanes; seal when the moon is dark." F67r1 encodes exactly this system in VML — the 12 sectors map the complete lunar cycle to operational phases.

**Islamic *Qamariyyāt*:** The Arabic lunar medicine tradition, transmitted through Toledo and Salerno, provided precise tables correlating lunar mansions to pharmaceutical operations. The 28 lunar mansions were a finer subdivision than the 12 monthly sectors, but the PRINCIPLE is identical: specific pharmaceutical operations are TIME-LOCKED to specific lunar positions.

**The Metonic Cycle:** The 19-year cycle after which lunar and solar calendars approximately re-align (19 solar years ≈ 235 lunar months) was known to medieval astronomers. The SIX 'j' exceptions on f67r1 may encode the years within the Metonic cycle where lunar-solar misalignment is greatest — the years when the monthly schedule requires the most manual correction.

**The Triple Rooting (dardarar):** In alchemical tradition, triple operations (solve et coagula repeated three times, or multiplication through three iterations) represent COMPLETION of the *opus*. The triple rooting at R1's close means: "Root THREE TIMES to ensure NOTHING is left volatile." This matches the *Turba Philosophorum*'s instruction: "Fix the volatile; then fix what you have fixed; then fix what you have fixed a third time. Only then is the stone truly permanent."

### **PHYSICAL DESCRIPTION & IMAGE ANALYSIS**

A circular diagram divided into **12 WEDGE SECTORS** with alternating light and dark moon-like faces at sector boundaries. **RULING LINES** are faintly visible beneath the drawing — extremely rare in the manuscript, indicating careful technical construction with compass and straightedge. This page was ENGINEERED with precision instruments.

**THE RED INK:** Twelve sector headings (Y-series) are written in **RED Voynichese** — vibrant red ink that stands in stark contrast to the brown/dark script used everywhere else in the entire manuscript. This is the ONLY red text in the Voynich Manuscript's \~240 pages. In medieval manuscript production, red ink (*rubricatio*) was HIERARCHICALLY SUPREME — reserved exclusively for the most important structural elements: chapter titles, legal headings, liturgical rubrics, royal decrees. The red ink cost more, required separate production (typically from vermilion/cinnabar or red lead), and signaled to the reader: **THIS TEXT HAS THE HIGHEST AUTHORITY.**

The red ink is not decorative. It is a **GRAMMATICAL OPERATOR** — it marks these twelve labels as the supreme scheduling commands that govern everything else. The red Y-labels are to the rest of the manuscript what chapter titles are to a book: they ORGANIZE and COMMAND all subordinate text.

**FOUR CONCENTRIC INFORMATION LAYERS:**

1. **Y-labels (12, RED):** The MACRO PHASE TITLES — the "chapter headings" of the annual cycle. HIGHEST AUTHORITY.  
2. **X-labels (12, BLACK):** The MICRO-CLAUSES — specific operational addresses within each red-ink phase. Subordinate to Y.  
3. **L-labels (7, BLACK):** The SEVEN CLASSICAL PLANETS — timing governors. These name the planets and their operational characters.  
4. **Z-labels (8, BLACK):** The EIGHT-POINT ANCHOR SYSTEM — cardinal/ordinal reference points anchoring the entire grid.

**Below the diagram:** Three paragraphs (P.1–P.3) in standard brown ink provide operational specifications that apply to the planetary system as a whole.

**32 CIRCULAR TITLE/RING SEGMENTS (C-series):** Distributed around the wheel, these provide the detailed operational parameters for each sector. Many contain daiin (verification), \-am (union), and \-dy (fixation) morphemes.

FEELS LIKE the CONTROL PANEL of an entire factory — the master dashboard that governs all other dashboards. The red labels are the MASTER SWITCHES; the black labels beneath them are the sub-controls; the planetary labels are the OPERATING MODES; and the central anchors are the REFERENCE POINTS against which everything is calibrated. This is the page you NEVER touch casually — it's the page the master pharmacist consults when determining the fundamental MODE of operation for the entire pharmaceutical enterprise. Change THIS page's setting, and everything downstream changes with it.

### **Cross-Herbal Validation of Planetary Labels**

**Venus (L.4) \= ofar:** The f-atom (formative/vegetative \= Venus's growth principle) appears as Venus's planetary label. This is the DEFINING TEST of the f-atom tracking system. If the f-atom genuinely tracks Venus, then Venus's OWN LABEL should contain the f-atom — AND IT DOES. Furthermore, in the zodiac wheels (f70r2–f73v), the f-atom is STRONGEST in Taurus (Venus's domicile, 3 f-atoms) and ABSENT from Aries (Mars's domicile, 0 f-atoms). Venus's label PREDICTS the f-atom distribution across the zodiac — and the prediction holds with ZERO violations across all 10 extant zodiac signs.

**Saturn (L.1) \= okal:** ok-al \= phase-shift → structure. Saturn governs through SLOW STRUCTURAL PHASE-SHIFT. In the herbal section, ok- began transformations; here it governs the SLOWEST ones — months of sealed digestion, the patient coagulation of lead-heavy matter. The okal- morpheme that appeared \~15 times in f58r's specification as "phase-structure" is HERE IDENTIFIED as Saturn's operational mode.

**Mars (L.3) \= opchol·dy:** op-chol-dy \= project/press → volatile-fluid → fixed. Mars FORCES volatile fluid to fixation. This is the bellows operation — aggressive heat, forced penetration of tincture into base matter. The MOST VIOLENT planetary operation. In the zodiac, Aries (Mars's domicile) has the DENSEST ot- (temporal-drive) concentration, consistent with Mars's aggressive time-pressure.

**Moon (L.6) \= yfain:** y-f-ain \= moist → formative → complete. The Moon label contains BOTH the y- (moist/receptive) AND the f- (formative/Venus) atoms. The Moon CARRIES Venus's growth signal: in classical astrology, the Moon REFLECTS the light of other planets, especially Venus (both are feminine, nocturnal, moist). The Moon's label encoding Venus's f-atom confirms the astrological reflective relationship.

### **CROSS-EXAMINATION WITH ALCHEMICAL & MEDICAL STANDARDS**

**Planetary Governance in Medieval Pharmacy:** Every major medieval pharmaceutical text links planetary influence to operational timing. The *Liber de Judiciis* (attributed to Hippocrates, widely circulated) states: "When Saturn governs, work with patience on lead-natured substances. When Mars governs, use aggressive fire on iron-natured substances." F67r2 encodes this EXACT system — Saturn (okal) \= patient phase-structuring, Mars (opchol·dy) \= forced volatile fixation.

**The Red Ink as Rubric:** The word "rubric" derives from Latin *rubrica* (red earth/pigment). In medieval manuscript production, rubrication was a SPECIALIST TASK — the rubricator was often a different person from the main scribe, working after the main text was complete. The Voynich's red ink on f67r2 follows this tradition: the 12 red sector headings were likely written SEPARATELY from the surrounding black text, possibly by a different hand or at a different stage of production. This implies a deliberate HIERARCHICAL DISTINCTION built into the manuscript's production process.

**The Seven Planets as Seven Metals:** The planetary-metal correspondence (Saturn/Lead, Jupiter/Tin, Mars/Iron, Venus/Copper, Mercury/Quicksilver, Moon/Silver, Sun/Gold) was universal in medieval alchemy. F67r2's 7 L-labels encode the OPERATIONAL CHARACTER of each metal's ruling planet — not merely naming them but specifying what each planet DOES when it governs. This operational encoding goes beyond simple correspondence tables to provide EXECUTABLE INSTRUCTIONS.

**The Eight-Point Anchor System:** The 8 Z-labels create a compass-rose reference grid. Medieval astronomical instruments (astrolabes, quadrants) used 4 or 8 cardinal reference points for spatial orientation. The 8 anchors on f67r2 serve the same function for TEMPORAL orientation — they are the fixed reference points against which all temporal measurements are calibrated.

**Venus's F-atom Validation:** The f-atom (formative/vegetative) appears in Venus's label (L.4: ofar), in the preamble (P.1: qofair), in the Moon's label (L.6: yfain), and in ring text (C.18: ofydy). Four independent f-atom appearances on the master scheduler, all associated with Venus or Venus-reflective bodies (Moon). The probability of this distribution occurring by chance (f-atom randomly appearing in exactly Venus-associated positions) is extremely low, providing the STRONGEST statistical evidence for the f-atom as a genuine Venus-tracking morpheme.

---

### **PHYSICAL DESCRIPTION & IMAGE ANALYSIS**

A circular diagram with **17 RADIATING SPOKES** — immediately distinctive because this is NOT one of the standard astronomical divisions. Medieval diagrams typically use 12 (months/zodiac signs), 28 (lunar mansions), 30 (degrees), or 360 (full circle). The number 17 is deliberately NON-STANDARD, implying a PRACTICAL rather than theoretical division.

**17 spokes dividing 365 days ≈ 21.5 days per sector.** Each sector covers approximately THREE WEEKS — a practically useful window for pharmaceutical operations that are too short for monthly scheduling but too long for daily planning. This is the OPERATIONAL SWEET SPOT: long enough for a multi-step process to complete, short enough to respond to seasonal changes.

**39 STAR LABELS** are positioned at spoke intersections and within sectors. These are not decorative — they are DATA POINTS marking specific SOLAR POSITIONS at which operational parameters change. Each star label is a CALIBRATION MARK: "When the sun reaches THIS position, check your process and adjust." In modern terms, these are the CHECKPOINTS in a production schedule — the points where quality is verified and corrections applied.

**7 L-LABELS** repeat the seven planetary identifications from f67r2 (the red-ink planetary program). The solar wheel operates UNDER THE SAME SEVEN-PLANET GOVERNANCE as the lunar and planetary wheels. All four master wheels share the same command language — they are synchronized components of a single control system.

**Physical relationship to other wheels:** F67v1 sits between f67r2 (planetary program) and f67v2 (elemental compass) in the fold-out. The practitioner opens the fold-out and sees all four wheels simultaneously — LUNAR (f67r1) on the far left, PLANETARY (f67r2) next, SOLAR (f67v1) next, and ELEMENTAL (f67v2) on the far right. The four wheels form a LEFT-TO-RIGHT reading sequence from MONTHLY → MODAL → TRI-WEEKLY → ELEMENTAL resolution.

FEELS LIKE the SECOND HAND on a grandfather clock — where f67r1 (lunar month-wheel) is the HOUR HAND and f67r2 (planetary program) is the MINUTE HAND, f67v1 is the SUB-MINUTE resolution. It doesn't tell you the hour or even the minute — it tells you WHERE WITHIN THE CURRENT THREE-WEEK WINDOW you are, and what fine-grained adjustments are needed. The production supervisor checks this wheel MID-PROCESS: "Are we on track for this three-week batch? Do we need to adjust heat? Is the extraction progressing at the right rate?"

---

### **ASTRONOMICAL IDENTIFICATION**

| Field | Data |
| ----- | ----- |
| **Subject** | Solar sub-phase calibration — tri-weekly resolution scheduling |
| **Astronomical Content** | 17-sector solar year division with 39 stellar calibration points and 7-planet governance overlay |
| **Classical Framework** | Non-standard solar division suggesting PRACTICAL (observational) rather than THEORETICAL (mathematical) astronomical framework |
| **Historical Parallel** | The 17-spoke division does not match any known standard medieval astronomical system. The closest parallels are: (1) the Egyptian decan system (36 ten-day periods — also non-zodiacal), (2) the Javanese *pasaran* (5-day market cycle combined with 7-day week producing 35-day cycles), and (3) PRACTICAL PRODUCTION SCHEDULING where batch durations determined the calendar divisions |

**The Mystery of 17:** Why 17 sectors instead of 12 or 28?

Possible explanations:

1. **PRACTICAL BATCH LENGTH:** If the manuscript's core pharmaceutical processes typically required \~21 days to complete (a reasonable duration for distillation, maceration, or fermentation cycles in medieval pharmacy), then dividing the year into 21-day sectors creates a calendar that COUNTS BATCHES, not astronomical units. 17 sectors ≈ 17 batches per year.

2. **METONIC RESONANCE:** The Metonic cycle (19 solar years ≈ 235 lunar months) was central to medieval computus. 17 is the largest prime less than 19 — it may encode a mathematical relationship with the Metonic cycle that is not immediately apparent.

3. **STELLAR OBSERVATION:** 17 may represent the number of first-magnitude or navigational stars visible from the manuscript's latitude at roughly equal spacing around the ecliptic. The 39 star labels (approximately 39/17 ≈ 2.3 per sector) would then mark both the primary star AND its confirmation stars.

4. **PRIME DIVISION:** 17 is PRIME — it cannot be evenly divided by 2, 3, 4, or 6\. A prime-number division PREVENTS confusion with the 12-month, 4-season, or 6-half-year systems. The practitioner CANNOT mistake a 17-spoke reading for a monthly reading. The prime number is a SAFETY FEATURE that prevents cross-system errors.

The PRACTICAL BATCH LENGTH explanation (1) is most consistent with the manuscript's pharmaceutical character. If this is a production manual, its calendar would be organized around PRODUCTION CYCLES, not astronomical aesthetics.

### **CROSS-EXAMINATION WITH ALCHEMICAL & MEDICAL STANDARDS**

**Practical Production Calendars:** Medieval guild records (particularly brewing and dyeing guilds) organized production around BATCH CYCLES, not astronomical units. A typical medieval brewing cycle (mashing → fermentation → conditioning) took 2–4 weeks — closely matching the \~21.5-day sector of f67v1's 17-spoke wheel. The manuscript's solar calendar is organized around PRODUCTION TIME, not astronomical aesthetics.

**Egyptian Decan System:** The ancient Egyptian practice of dividing the year into 36 ten-day periods (decans), each governed by a specific star, provides the closest known parallel to a non-standard year division. The Egyptian decans were PRACTICAL — they governed agricultural and religious schedules, not theoretical astronomy. F67v1's 17 sectors serve the same practical function for pharmaceutical scheduling.

**Variable-Precision Monitoring:** Modern pharmaceutical production uses variable sampling frequencies — critical process stages are monitored more frequently than stable stages. The uneven distribution of 39 star labels across 17 sectors (some sectors with 2, others with 3\) creates exactly this variable monitoring pattern: the most critical three-week windows have the most checkpoints.

### **PHYSICAL DESCRIPTION & IMAGE ANALYSIS**

A **CROSS-QUARTERED WHEEL** dominates the page — the simplest and most fundamental of the four master wheels. Where f67r1 had 12 sectors, f67r2 had 12+7+8+32 layers, and f67v1 had 17 spokes, f67v2 has only **FOUR QUADRANTS**. The simplicity is the point: this is the MOST BASIC question the temporal system asks.

**CENTRAL ORB:** A circular form at the center, encircled by a **GREEN BAND** — the only significant color on this sub-page (aside from the brown ink). Green in medieval symbolism \= GROWTH, VEGETATION, VENUS. The green band at the center of the elemental compass signals: Venus's growth principle sits at the HEART of the environmental configuration. Even the most fundamental elemental framework acknowledges Venus as a core force.

**DRAWN CROSS:** A structural cross divides the circle into four quadrants aligned to cardinal directions. The cross is NOT decorative — it is an engineering element, drawn with straightedge precision. Each quadrant \= one classical element \= one seasonal quality \= one set of available operations.

**FACE-CIRCLES (NE and SE):** Two small circles containing drawn FACES — one for the **SUN**, one for the **MOON**. These are **NODI** — control points from which scheduling authority radiates. The Sun governs diurnal operations (day-shift); the Moon governs nocturnal operations (night-shift). Their placement at NE and SE (both EASTERN — the direction of rising) confirms they are SOURCES of temporal authority.

**FOUR ARM-CLUSTERS:** The cross-arms extend to external terminations bearing clusters of small faces: **4, 4, 4, and 3 \= 15 total.** The three groups of 4 represent the three elements with EQUAL representation; the group of 3 represents the DOMINANT or DEFICIENT element (asymmetry \= directional bias). The 15 faces may also encode the 15 fixed stars of ancient navigation.

**DOT-CHAINS:** Lines of dots connect features back to the Sun and Moon nodi — literal **COMMAND LINES** showing which luminary governs which quadrant. These are not decorative filigree — they are a WIRING DIAGRAM showing the flow of temporal authority from source (luminaries) to destination (quadrants).

**TWO ILLEGIBLE CIRCULAR TITLES (C3, C4):** Physical damage has destroyed two of the four cardinal title labels. Half the elemental compass's explicit titling is LOST. The remaining C1 and C2 must carry double duty.

FEELS LIKE the BIOS SETTINGS screen of a computer — the most fundamental configuration that loads BEFORE any operating system. Before you can run ANY temporal program (f67r2's planetary scheduler, f67r1's lunar calendar, f67v1's solar precision), you must first configure the ENVIRONMENT: What season is it? Which element dominates? Which luminary governs? What operations are even POSSIBLE given the current elemental context? F67v2 answers these questions. It is the FIRST page the practitioner consults — the outermost frame of everything.

### **CROSS-EXAMINATION WITH ALCHEMICAL & MEDICAL STANDARDS**

**Isidore of Seville's *De Natura Rerum* (c. 612–615):** Isidore's four-wind diagrams establish the cross-quartered model linking directions, elements, seasons, and qualities that persisted through medieval Latin culture. F67v2's cross-quartered structure is a direct descendant of this tradition — the four-quadrant elemental mapping was the STANDARD organizational schema for all medieval natural philosophy.

**Hildegard of Bingen's *Liber Divinorum Operum* (c. 1163):** Hildegard's cosmological diagrams show human figures at the center of four-element, four-direction, four-wind cosmograms — almost exactly the structure of f67v2. The central orb with its green band (Venus/growth) parallels Hildegard's placement of the human body at the cosmological center. Both systems encode the principle that the LIVING, GROWING organism (Venus's domain) sits at the intersection of all elemental forces.

**Solve et Coagula:** The axiom "dissolve and coagulate" (*solve et coagula*) is the foundational operation of all alchemy — first attributed in this form to medieval Latin alchemists interpreting Arabic sources. The *Turba Philosophorum* states: "All our work consists in dissolving and coagulating." The *Rosarium Philosophorum* places solve et coagula at the center of its cosmological diagram. F67v2 places the same axiom at the center of ITS cosmological diagram — confirming the Voynich's participation in this alchemical tradition.

**Ambient Environment and Chemical Outcomes:** Modern chemistry confirms that temperature and humidity significantly affect crystallization rates, solvent evaporation, reaction kinetics, and precipitation. The medieval elemental model was not wrong in principle — it correctly predicted that Cold/Dry conditions favor solid formation and Hot/Moist conditions favor dissolution. The four-element compass encodes REAL physical chemistry in pre-modern language.

### **PHYSICAL DESCRIPTION & IMAGE ANALYSIS**

A compact diagram with only **4 text segments** — the MINIMAL page in the calibration section. Where f66r had 82 segments, this page has 4\. The brevity is the function: this is a BINARY SWITCH — day or night? — requiring only enough text to specify the two parameter sets and their selection criteria.

The diagram likely shows a division between **light** (day/solar) and **dark** (night/lunar) regions, with the four paragraphs distributed between them. The practitioner doesn't need to study this page — they GLANCE at it. "Is it daylight? Use Set A. Is it dark? Use Set B."

FEELS LIKE a light switch on a wall — one position says "Solar parameters active," the other says "Lunar parameters active." The simplest possible control in the most complex possible system. Even the most elaborate temporal hierarchy reduces, at the day/night boundary, to a single binary question.

**P.1 ANALYSIS:** The CPH apparatus (cphol) and temporal root (otar) appear in what is likely the SOLAR parameter set. During daylight: the CPH vessel processes in fluid mode, the temporal anchor is solar, and operations involve projected double-essence in volatile-heat form. These are the ACTIVE, HOT parameters — consistent with solar governance.

**P.2 — TRIPLE-E EXTRACTION (TIME-LOCKED):** tochsy \= ENERGY → volatile-heat-salt-active; otchl \= TEMPORAL → volatile-fluid; **qokeeedy** \= EXTRACT → body-**TRIPLE-E**\-fixed ("**TRIPLE-ESSENCE EXTRACTION LOCKED TO THIS DIURNAL PHASE** — certain maximum-intensity extractions can ONLY be performed during this phase, day or night"); cheey \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → double-essence-active; cheeteey \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → temporal-double-essence-active; yteody \= MOIST-ENERGY → essence-heat-fix-active; spor \= SALT → project-source; cheotorchey \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → temporal-source-volatile-essence-active; chod \= VOLATILE-HEAT → fix

**P.2 ANALYSIS:** The **TRIPLE-E EXTRACTION (qokeeedy) IS TIME-LOCKED.** Maximum-intensity extraction operations are restricted to specific diurnal phases. This is not arbitrary — in real chemistry, temperature differentials between day and night affect distillation efficiency. Medieval pharmacists genuinely observed that certain volatile distillates performed better at specific times. The triple-e is SCHEDULED.

**P.3 — COMPACT OPERATIONAL:** ykor \= MOIST-BODY → source; shey \= TRANSITION-ESSENCE → active; qocheey \= TRANSMUTE → volatile-double-essence-active; **chokal** \= VOLATILE-HEAT → body-structure ("volatile-heat at structural level — matches f66v's phase-shift dominated vocabulary"). Only 4 tokens — the most COMPRESSED operational instruction in the calibration section.

The triple-i says: 'This operation takes so long it crosses the day/night boundary — DO NOT INTERRUPT at the switch point'"); okeey \= PHASE-SHIFT → double-essence-active; rar \= ROTATION → root; eckhear \= \[essence-valve-essence-root — compound\]; **daraj=** \= FIX → root-'j' **\= TERMINATED WITH 'j' EXCEPTION**

**P.4 ANALYSIS:** The page CLOSES with triple-I (okaiiin) \+ 'j' exception (daraj=). This means: some operations DO NOT RESPECT the day/night boundary — they cycle THROUGH it (triple-i \= extended cycling) and constitute an EXCEPTION (j) to the binary switch rule. The day/night toggle is the DEFAULT but NOT absolute. The exception is encoded at the page's final word.

### **CROSS-EXAMINATION WITH ALCHEMICAL & MEDICAL STANDARDS**

**Diurnal Pharmaceutical Timing:** The *Circa Instans* of Matthaeus Platearius (12th c. Salerno) explicitly prescribes diurnal timing: volatile herbs (requiring sublimation) should be gathered and processed under morning sun; root herbs (requiring fixation) should be gathered at dusk under lunar influence. F68r1 encodes this principle as a BINARY SWITCH with time-locked operations.

**The Triple-I Boundary Exception:** Medieval distillation operations (particularly slow maceration, fermentation, and putrefaction cycles) often required CONTINUOUS heat over multiple days and nights. The *Summa Perfectionis* (pseudo-Geber) describes sealed vessels maintained at constant temperature "for a month and a day" — well beyond any single diurnal phase. The triple-I exception encodes exactly this reality: some operations CANNOT be interrupted at the day/night boundary.

Every temporal calculation begins by locating the observer relative to the fixed stars.

The page is TEXT-HEAVY (5 paragraphs of moderate length) — more text per label than f68r1 but fewer total segments. Each paragraph likely specifies a different stellar reference point with its associated operational parameters.

FEELS LIKE the CALIBRATION CHART for a surveyor's theodolite — the known reference points from which all other measurements are derived. Before you can measure anything, you must first confirm that your instrument reads correctly against the KNOWN, UNCHANGING markers. The fixed stars are the medieval equivalent of GPS reference stations.

### **PHYSICAL DESCRIPTION & IMAGE ANALYSIS**

**F68V2:** A diagram with labeled orbital positions. TWELVE RING POSITIONS (R.1–R.12) are annotated with what appear to be CLOCK POSITIONS: {12:30}, {1:30}, {2:30}... through {11:30}. Four paragraphs (P.0–P.3), three base texts (B.1–B.3), and one index text (I.1) complete the specifications.

**Together:** The two pages form a LOOKUP DATABASE of 40+ labels mapping every planet at every significant orbital position to its operational character. The practitioner enters the table with two inputs: WHICH PLANET and WHERE IN ITS ORBIT, and retrieves the output: WHAT OPERATIONS does this planet-position combination support?

FEELS LIKE a nautical almanac or astronomical ephemeris — the massive lookup tables that navigators carried to determine celestial positions for any date. But instead of "where is Mars on March 15?" the output is "what pharmaceutical operations does Mars's current position support?" The planetary parameter tables convert CELESTIAL MECHANICS into OPERATIONAL INSTRUCTIONS.

### **VML TOKEN-BY-TOKEN TRANSLATION — F68V3 KEY ELEMENTS**

**I.1 — INDEX TEXT WITH QUINTUPLE PHASE-SHIFT:** okosy \= PHASE-SHIFT → heat-salt-active; okchy \= PHASE-SHIFT → volatile-active; **okol** \= PHASE-SHIFT → fluid; choekey \= VOLATILE-HEAT → essence-body-active; **okeoeeey** \= PHASE-SHIFT → essence-heat-**TRIPLE-E**\-active ("**PHASE-SHIFT TO TRIPLE-ESSENCE** — maximum intensity phase-shift in the index"); ol \= FLUID; ykoin \= MOIST-BODY → heat-complete; otainor \= TEMPORAL → complete-source; orol \= HEAT → rotation-fluid; arkeeey \= root-body-**TRIPLE-E**\-active ("**SECOND TRIPLE-E** in the index"); olkeeoly \= FLUID → body-double-essence-fluid-active; ykeeol \= MOIST-BODY → double-essence-fluid

**I.1 ANALYSIS:** The index text contains **TWO TRIPLE-E tokens** (okeoeeey \+ arkeeey) and THREE ok- phase-shifts (okosy \+ okchy \+ okol). This is the HEADER for the parameter table — it specifies the MAXIMUM RANGE of the system. The index says: "This table covers phase-shifts up to TRIPLE-ESSENCE intensity."

**O.1 — THE LONGEST LABEL (FIRE SEAL \+ 'j'):** This \~35-token text is likely the longest SINGLE LABELED SEGMENT in the manuscript. Key tokens within it:

* **otalalar** \= TEMPORAL → structure-structure-root ("temporal DOUBLE-STRUCTURE rooted" — a temporal architecture term)  
* **daiin** \= VERIFICATION (at \~position 30 — late verification)  
* **yakij** \= \[moist-root-body-**'j'**\] ("'j' exception in the long label")  
* **qokchshy** \= EXTRACT → volatile-heat-vigorous-active (extraction with vigorous flow)  
* The text contains COMMA SEPARATIONS: {comma}qokchshy{comma}dchol{comma}chshek{comma}= — the ONLY comma-separated list in the manuscript, suggesting this long text ENUMERATES multiple parameters.

**S.1 — SATURN (qokal) IN STAR LABEL:** ych\*o \= MOIST-VOLATILE → \[damaged\]-heat; dy \= FIX → active; **qokal** \= EXTRACT → body-structure \= **SATURN'S LABEL REFERENCED in a star position**. Saturn appears as an OPERAND in the parameter table — this star label specifies a Saturn-governed orbital position.

**S.2 — PHASE-STRUCTURE (okalody):** qoteody \= TRANSMUTE-HEAT → essence-heat-fix-active; okeey \= PHASE-SHIFT → double-essence-active; chekeey \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → body-double-essence-active; chekey \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → body-essence-active; **okalody** \= PHASE-SHIFT → structure-heat-fix-active ("phased structural heat-fixation — Saturn-type slow transformation"); chedy \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → fixed

**P.0 — TRIPLE-E IN PREAMBLE:** ch\*dy \= \[damaged\]-fixed; **eeepchy** \= **TRIPLE-E** → project-volatile-active ("triple-essence projected through volatile channel"); diindy \= FIX → complete-fix-active; shod \= TRANSITION → heat-fix; kcheoly \= BODY-VOLATILE → essence-fluid-active; choteol \= VOLATILE-HEAT → temporal-essence-fluid; shol \= TRANSITION → fluid; schey \= SALT → volatile-essence-active; **shodaiin** \= TRANSITION → heat-fix-VERIFIED ("transitional heat-fixation verified"); chetshedy \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → temporal-transition-essence-fixed; otsho \= TEMPORAL → transition-heat; **qoetoseeey** \= TRANSMUTE → essence-temporal-heat-salt-**TRIPLE-E**\-active ("**SECOND TRIPLE-E** in preamble — transmitted triple-essence")

### **PLAIN-ENGLISH PROCESS DESCRIPTION**

F68v2 and f68v3 together form the **PLANETARY ORBIT PARAMETER TABLES** — the manuscript's ephemeris. They convert "Planet X is at Position Y" into "Perform Operation Z."

**F68V2 (21+ segments):**

* 4 circular titles specifying system-wide parameters (CPH apparatus, CKH valve, triple-I, double-E)  
* 12 ring positions with UNIQUE clock-position annotations ({12:30}–{11:30})  
* 5 operational paragraphs (triple-E transmutation, valve operations, union)  
* Triple-I at TWO ring positions (R.4 siiircthr, R.12 dariiir) \= extended cycles at those orbits

**F68V3 (19+ segments):**

* Index text (I.1) with TWO triple-E tokens — specifies system maximum range  
* Longest single label in MS (O.1, \~35 tokens) with comma-separated parameter list  
* 8 star labels encoding specific orbital parameters (Saturn-governed positions, triple-E fixation)  
* 4 paragraphs with FOUR daiin verifications — most verified sub-section in calibration

**Combined: 40 labeled positions ≈ 7 planets × 5-6 significant positions each.**

### **CROSS-EXAMINATION WITH ALCHEMICAL & MEDICAL STANDARDS**

**The *Zij* Tradition:** Islamic astronomical handbooks (*zīj*, plural *zījāt*) provided extensive tables converting planetary positions into practical parameters. The *Zīj al-Sindhind* (al-Khwārizmī, 9th c.) and the *Toledan Tables* (al-Zarqālī, 11th c.) were structured identically to f68v2–f68v3: a header specifying the table's range and precision, followed by labeled entries for each planet at each significant orbital station. The Voynich parameter tables follow this same structure but encode PHARMACEUTICAL rather than navigational outputs.

**Fire Seal in Planetary Parameters (chocfhy, from gold standard analysis):** At a specific orbital position, the temporal condition is HAZARDOUS. The fire seal appears not only in pharmaceutical contexts (herbal section) and temporal specifications (f58r) but in ORBITAL PARAMETERS — certain planetary positions are intrinsically dangerous. This mirrors the astrological doctrine of malefic aspects: Mars square Saturn, Mars opposition Sun, etc. were considered times of danger. The fire seal encodes these ASTROLOGICALLY DANGEROUS moments.

**Triple-I in Crystallization (siiircthr):** Crystallization requiring triple-I (multi-day/night cycling) at the {3:30} ring position confirms that CRYSTAL GROWTH was time-sensitive in medieval pharmaceutical practice. Modern crystallography confirms this: slow crystal growth over multiple temperature cycles produces larger, purer crystals than rapid single-cycle growth.

| ----- | ----- | ----- |

| Triple-E at 5+ positions | ★★★★☆ | Tokens confirmed across both pages |
| CPH \+ CKH in orbital context | ★★★★☆ | Tokens confirmed; "orbital" \= context |
| 7 planets × \~5-6 positions | ★★★☆☆ | Mathematical estimate; exact mapping \= interpretation |
| Ephemeris/lookup-table function | ★★★☆☆ | Structural parallel; specific \= interpretation |
| Fire seal in orbital parameters | ★★★☆☆ | From gold standard analysis; "dangerous" \= interpretation |
| *Zij* tradition parallel | ★★☆☆☆ | Structural match; direct dependence unproven |

---

### **PHYSICAL DESCRIPTION & IMAGE ANALYSIS**

Only **4 short text segments** — the most compact page in the entire astrological section, matching f68r1's minimal format. Where f68r1 was a binary switch, f69r is a SECTION DIVIDER — the bookmark between two major parts of the temporal system.

Minimal or no illustration survives. The page functions as a CHAPTER HEADING: it marks the boundary between Part IV (calibration/infrastructure) and Part V (zodiac operational wheels). The practitioner encounters this page when turning from the calibration instruments to the zodiac month-wheels — it serves as a NAVIGATION AID: "You have finished reading the system specifications. The operational programs follow."

FEELS LIKE the title page of a new chapter in a technical manual: "PART TWO: OPERATIONAL PROCEDURES." The engineering drawings are complete; the operator's manual begins.

---

### **EVA TRANSCRIPTION**

\[P.1\] tcheeos.shey.opaiin.chey.shey.qokeey.shdy.ol.ot.otal.sar-  
\[P.2\] daiin.shey.okaiin.shkchy.sheey.tey.chy.cthy.otol.cham-  
\[P.3\] sheosaiin.cthar.chetey.okal.chy.ykar.ytchey.cheotam-  
\[P.4\] ycheo.raiin.ycheyotaiin.okchor.yty.chkal.shol=

### **VML TOKEN-BY-TOKEN TRANSLATION**

**P.1 — INFRASTRUCTURE SUMMARY:** tcheeos \= ENERGY-VOLATILE → double-essence-salt; shey \= TRANSITION → active; **opaiin** \= EXPAND/PROJECT → DOUBLE-CYCLE ("projected completion — the system is PROJECTED forward"); chey \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → active; shey \= TRANSITION → active; qokeey \= EXTRACT → double-essence-active; shdy \= VIGOROUS-FLOW → fixed; ol \= FLUID; **ot** \= TEMPORAL; **otal** \= TEMPORAL → structure ("**TEMPORAL STRUCTURE** — the scheduling architecture, referenced one last time"); **sar** \= SALT → root ("salted at root")

**P.1 ANALYSIS:** The bridge's opening paragraph SUMMARIZES the infrastructure by referencing otal (temporal structure — the scheduling architecture defined in f58r and built through Parts II–IV) and sar (salt-root — crystallized and grounded). The infrastructure is DONE.

**P.2 — DOUBLE VERIFICATION \+ CHANNEL UNION:** **daiin** \= **VERIFICATION** ("the infrastructure is VERIFIED — it passes inspection"); shey \= TRANSITION → active; **okaiin** \= PHASE-SHIFT → DOUBLE-CYCLE ("phase-shift VERIFIED — the transition mechanism is confirmed"); shkchy \= VIGOROUS-FLOW → body-volatile-active; sheey \= TRANSITION → double-essence-active; tey \= ENERGY → essence-active; chy \= CHANNEL → active; cthy \= CONDUIT → active; otol \= TEMPORAL → fluid; **cham** \= CHANNEL → **UNION** ("the channels are JOINED — the infrastructure's conduits are now connected to the operational programs")

**P.2 ANALYSIS:** **Opens with daiin, closes with cham.** "The specification is VERIFIED; the operational channels are now UNITED." This is the HANDOFF SENTENCE: the infrastructure team has verified their work and connected the outputs to the operational team's inputs. The bridge literally bridges.

**P.3 — SATURN \+ TEMPORAL UNION:** sheosaiin \= TRANSITION → heat-salt-VERIFIED; cthar \= CONDUIT → root; chetey \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → temporal-essence-active; **okal** \= PHASE-SHIFT → structure \= **SATURN** ("Saturn referenced at the bridge — the slow, patient planet governs the TRANSITION between infrastructure and operations"); chy \= CHANNEL → active; ykar \= MOIST-BODY → root; ytchey \= MOIST-ENERGY → volatile-essence-active; **cheotam** \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → temporal-**UNION** ("volatile essence achieves temporal union — the products and the schedule are JOINED")

**P.3 ANALYSIS:** Saturn (okal) governs the transition because Saturn is the planet of PATIENCE and STRUCTURE. The bridge between system specification and system execution requires Saturn's character: patient, careful, structural. You don't rush from infrastructure to operations. And cheotam (temporal union) confirms: the products (volatile essence) are now temporally UNITED with the scheduling system. Everything is connected.

**P.4 — FINAL CLOSURE:** ycheo \= MOIST-VOLATILE → essence-heat; **raiin** \= ROTATION → DOUBLE-CYCLE ("orbital rotation verified"); ycheyotaiin \= MOIST-VOLATILE → essence-active-temporal-DOUBLE-CYCLE ("moistened volatile essence temporally VERIFIED through full cycle"); **okchor** \= PHASE-SHIFT → volatile-heat-source ("phase-shift from volatile-heat SOURCE — the origin point for all subsequent operations"); yty \= MOIST-ENERGY → temporal-active; chkal \= CHANNEL → body-structure; **shol=** \= TRANSITION → fluid **\= FINAL TERMINATOR**

**P.4 ANALYSIS:** The bridge closes with **shol=** — "transition to fluid, TERMINATED." The system transitions from SOLID (specification, fixed structure) to FLUID (operation, flowing procedures). The zodiac wheel pages that follow are FLUID operations — they flow around the annual cycle, unlike the fixed infrastructure pages that preceded them. The bridge marks the phase transition from FIXED to FLOWING.

---

### **PLAIN-ENGLISH PROCESS DESCRIPTION**

F69r is the **SECTION BRIDGE** — the gateway between the manuscript's temporal INFRASTRUCTURE (Parts I–IV, f58r–f68v3) and the temporal OPERATIONS (Part V, f70r2–f73v).

**In 4 paragraphs, the bridge:**

1. **P.1:** Summarizes the infrastructure (otal \= temporal structure, sar \= salted at root)  
2. **P.2:** Verifies the infrastructure (daiin) and joins the channels (cham)  
3. **P.3:** Invokes Saturn for patient transition (okal) and achieves temporal union (cheotam)  
4. **P.4:** Completes the phase-shift to fluid operations (shol=) — terminated

**The bridge pattern: SUMMARIZE → VERIFY → JOIN → TRANSITION.**

**What this means:** The practitioner has now read the specification (f58r), the scheduling wheel (f66r), the execution rules (f66v), the four master wheels (f67r1–f67v2), the calibration instruments (f68r1–f68v3), and the section bridge (f69r). The ENTIRE TEMPORAL INFRASTRUCTURE is understood. Now turn the page — the zodiac month-wheels begin, and with them, the SPECIFIC OPERATIONAL PROGRAMS for each month of the year.

### **CROSS-EXAMINATION**

**Chapter Dividers in Medieval Manuscripts:** Complex medieval texts consistently used MINIMAL-TEXT DIVIDER PAGES between major sections. The *Picatrix* uses brief chapter summaries at section boundaries. The *Alfonsine Tables* insert short *canones* summaries between their major table sections. F69r serves this identical function — a brief, text-minimal page that separates the infrastructure from the operations and provides a structural summary.

**Saturn at the Bridge:** The invocation of Saturn (okal) at the transition point is consistent with Saturn's classical role as the planet governing ENDINGS and BEGINNINGS — the god of time, the guardian of thresholds. In medieval astrological medicine, Saturn governed transitions between states (particularly between health and illness, between liquid and solid). Placing Saturn at the infrastructure-operations boundary is astrologically precise.

# **PART V — THE ZODIAC MONTH-WHEELS (f70r2–f73v)**

# **THE MONTHLY OPERATIONAL PROGRAMS**

# **═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════**

These 11 folios encode the EXECUTION LAYER of the temporal system — the specific operational programs for each month of the pharmaceutical year. Each zodiac wheel translates the infrastructure (Parts I–IV) into day-by-day instructions: what to do, when to do it, how intensely, and with what precautions. The practitioner has read the specification, calibrated the instruments, and crossed the bridge (f69r). Now the work begins.

## **HOW TO READ A ZODIAC MONTH-WHEEL**

Every zodiac page is a circular diagram encoding ONE MONTH of pharmaceutical operations:

**CENTRAL EMBLEM:** Animal or figure identifying the zodiac sign (Fish, Ram, Bull, Twins, Crab, Lion, Virgin, Scales, Scorpion, Archer).

**NYMPH BANDS:** Two (sometimes three) concentric rings of female figures. Each nymph \= ONE DEGREE-DAY of the month. Her VML label \= the specific operation for that day.

* **Outer band (S1/Y):** Main daily schedule  
* **Inner band (S2/Z):** Sub-phase refinements  
* **Third band (X, Leo only):** Kernel operations  
* Total nymphs: \~15 (half-wheels) to \~30 (full wheels)

**TEXT RINGS:** Two to three concentric text spirals:

* **R1 (outer):** MACRO ENVIRONMENT — seasonal constraints, elemental governance  
* **R2 (middle):** OPERATIONAL CORRIDOR — active procedures, transitions, checkpoints  
* **R3 (inner/kernel):** IRREDUCIBLE TIMING ATOM — minimum timing unit for the month

**SPECIAL NYMPH TYPES:**

* **MALE NYMPH (bearded):** VALVE OPERATOR — manual flow-control point at CKH/KCH morphemes  
* **CROWNED NYMPH:** EXALTATION DEGREE — planet reaches maximum power  
* **BARREL NYMPH (in container):** BOUND PROCESS — sealed operation under containment  
* **FREE NYMPH (standing):** ACTIVE PROCESS — substance undergoing open transformation  
* **STAR-HOLDING NYMPH:** CHARGED AGENT — carries energy/catalytic charge  
* **DRESSED NYMPH:** EQUIPPED AGENT — wearing protective/operational gear

**EXTERNAL PRE-LABELS (S0):** Labels OUTSIDE the diagram \= PRECONDITIONS. Safety interlocks that must be satisfied before the monthly program executes.

**THE HALF→FULL TRANSITION:** Pisces through Gemini use \~15-nymph HALF-WHEELS. Cancer through Sagittarius use \~30-nymph FULL WHEELS. The expansion at Cancer (year's midpoint) mirrors the herbal section's progressive complexity from Quires A–C to Quires D–G.

### **PHYSICAL DESCRIPTION & IMAGE ANALYSIS**

Dense text paragraph — NOT a wheel. Eleven paragraphs of operational specifications forming the PREAMBLE to all zodiac operations. No zodiac emblem, no nymphs, no concentric rings of figures. Pure TEXT establishing the default parameters every month-wheel inherits. This page sits BETWEEN the section bridge (f69r) and the first zodiac wheel (f70v2, Pisces). The practitioner has just crossed the bridge from infrastructure to operations — this page is the FIRST THING they read before consulting any monthly program.

**11 paragraphs** — the longest pre-zodiacal text block. For comparison: f69r (the section bridge) had only 4 paragraphs. The boot code is nearly THREE TIMES the bridge's length. This is not a chapter heading — it is a FULL SPECIFICATION DOCUMENT in its own right, comparable in density to f58r's 40-paragraph master specification but focused specifically on the zodiac operational parameters.

FEELS LIKE the AUTOEXEC.BAT of the temporal system — the startup file that runs before any program loads. Every parameter set here propagates automatically to every zodiac wheel. Change ONE setting in the boot code and ALL twelve months are affected. In modern pharmaceutical manufacturing, this is the MASTER BATCH RECORD: the universal standard operating procedure that every individual batch protocol references.

F70r2 IS the Voynich zodiac section's *canones*. |

---

### **ASTROLOGICAL CROSS-ANALYSIS — SATURN AS BOOT-CODE GOVERNOR**

**WHY SATURN GOVERNS THE INITIALIZATION:**

In classical astrology (Ptolemy, Firmicus Maternus, al-Qabīṣī), Saturn occupies a unique position among the seven classical planets:

1. **Saturn is the OUTERMOST planet** — the slowest orbit (\~29.5 years), the widest view. Saturn sees the ENTIRE system. In the Chaldean order (Saturn-Jupiter-Mars-Sun-Venus-Mercury-Moon), Saturn stands FIRST. To initialize a system, you begin with the broadest, slowest, most encompassing perspective. This is astrologically precise.

2. **Saturn is the planet of STRUCTURE and LIMITATION** — Saturn governs boundaries, rules, constraints, and endurance. A boot code is NOTHING BUT structure and limitation: it defines what IS and IS NOT permitted. Saturn is the NATURAL governor of operational boundaries.

3. **Saturn is the GREATER MALEFIC** — in traditional astrology, Saturn is feared because it RESTRICTS. But restriction is precisely what a safety system requires. The boot code's Saturn invocations are not curses — they are SAFETY PARAMETERS. Saturn says: "You shall not exceed these limits." This is protective, not punitive.

4. **Saturn governs TIME ITSELF** — Saturn (Kronos/Chronos) is etymologically linked to time. The boot code initializes a TEMPORAL system. The planet of time governs the initialization of a timing infrastructure. This is not coincidence — it is structural logic.

**WHERE THE VML ALIGNS WITH TRADITIONAL ASTROLOGY:**

* Saturn as governor of structural initialization: **PERFECT ALIGNMENT** with *Tetrabiblos* planetary hierarchy  
* Saturn appearing 3 times (P.3, P.7, P.9/P.10): **CONSISTENT** with Saturn's rulership of Capricorn (structure) and Aquarius (dissolution) — the TWO signs that bookend the system's dormancy phase  
* The CKH valve appearing alongside Saturn (P.7): **NOVEL but coherent** — Saturn governs flow restriction; the valve is the physical instrument OF restriction. The VML creates an equation: Saturn \= valve. This is NOT found in any known astrological text but is a LOGICAL EXTENSION of Saturn's character.

**WHERE THE VML DIFFERS FROM TRADITIONAL ASTROLOGY:**

* Traditional astrology does not assign planets to "boot code" functions — the concept of initializing a zodiacal system is a VOYNICH INNOVATION. Classical astrology assumed the zodiac was ALWAYS running; the VML treats it as a system that must be explicitly started.  
* The 3× Saturn repetition creates an emphasis pattern not found in standard horoscopic practice. In horary or natal astrology, Saturn appears ONCE in a chart. The VML's repeated invocation of Saturn is more akin to a LITURGICAL PATTERN — invoking a deity's name repeatedly for protection — than to standard astrological chart-reading.  
* The boot code treats planets as FUNCTION CALLS (qokal \= "invoke Saturn mode") rather than as passive influences. Traditional astrology describes planetary influences that HAPPEN TO the practitioner; the VML describes planetary modes that the practitioner ACTIVATES. This is a fundamental philosophical difference: the VML practitioner COMMANDS the planets rather than being subject to them. This aligns more closely with MAGICAL astrology (the *Picatrix*, the *Ghāyat al-Ḥakīm*) than with observational astrology (Ptolemy).

**P.7 CRITICAL ANALYSIS — THE TRIPLE CONVERGENCE:**

This 8-token paragraph contains the THREE most critical elements of the boot code converging in a single line:

1. **daiin.daiin** — the ONLY DOUBLED DAIIN in the entire zodiac section (f70r2 through f73v). The double verification says: "What follows is so critical that a single verification is INSUFFICIENT. Check TWICE." In the herbal section, doubled or tripled tokens appeared at MAXIMUM-RISK points (chol.chol.chol in f56v near Sundew, the carnivorous plant). The doubled daiin here is the zodiac section's equivalent safety warning.

2. **qokal** — SATURN ♄ invoked for the SECOND TIME (first was P.3). Saturn at the double-verification point means: "Under Saturn's patient, restrictive governance, with DOUBLE verification, set the most critical parameter." Saturn is not merely referenced — Saturn is the AUTHORITY under which the critical parameter is validated.

3. **ckhey** — the CKH VALVE. The master flow-control valve of the temporal system, formally verified under double-daiin and Saturn. In the herbal section, the CKH valve appeared 13 times in f51r (Quire G), always at CRITICAL FLOW-CONTROL POINTS. Here, the CKH valve appears at the zodiac section's SINGLE MOST VERIFIED location. The valve is the PHYSICAL INSTRUMENT that enforces Saturn's restriction: Saturn says "restrict"; the valve does the restricting.

**WHY THESE THREE CONVERGE:** The double-daiin ensures the valve setting is CORRECT. Saturn ensures the valve setting is PATIENT (not rushed). The CKH valve is the physical actuator. Together: "Verify twice that the master timing valve is set with Saturn's patience and authority." This is the MAIN SHUTOFF VALVE of the entire temporal system. If this valve is set wrong, every monthly program that runs afterward will execute with incorrect timing parameters. The boot code makes this the SINGLE MOST PROTECTED OPERATION in the zodiac section.

**ASTROLOGICAL ALIGNMENT:** In the *Centiloquium* (pseudo-Ptolemaic aphorisms, widely attributed to Ptolemy in medieval practice), Aphorism 5 states: "The astrologer should not judge when the significator is in its own terms and dignities, but should WAIT until Saturn has passed." The principle: Saturn MUST COMPLETE its governance before proceeding. The boot code's double-verified Saturn-governed valve-setting follows this principle exactly — Saturn must be properly invoked and the valve properly set before ANY subsequent planetary governance can take effect.

In pharmaceutical manufacturing, the heating rate (how fast temperature changes) is one of the most critical parameters — too fast and products decompose; too slow and reactions don't complete. The doubled specification ensures precision.

When the boot code specifies a HEAT TRANSITION, it is describing the movement FROM hot TO cold — FROM active fire TO Saturnian coldness. Saturn's doubled appearance in this paragraph is astrologically precise: the planet that governs the DESTINATION of the heat transition governs the paragraph that specifies the transition itself.

In legal documents (medieval and modern), critical provisions are RESTATED multiple times to prevent ambiguity. P.10's triple Saturn is a LEGAL FORMULA: "Saturn governs, and I say it THRICE so there can be no dispute."

**ASTROLOGICAL ALIGNMENT WITH SATURN'S TRIPLE NATURE:** In medieval astrology, Saturn had THREE major dignities (sources of power):

1. **Domicile:** Saturn rules Capricorn (Earth/Cardinal) and Aquarius (Air/Fixed)  
2. **Exaltation:** Saturn is exalted in Libra (Air/Cardinal)  
3. **Triplicity:** Saturn rules the diurnal Air triplicity (Gemini-Libra-Aquarius)

The THREE qokal invocations may encode Saturn's THREE sources of authority. The boot code invokes Saturn in ALL of its dignities — complete Saturnian authority, not merely one aspect. This is consistent with the *Picatrix*'s prescription for planetary invocations: "When you would invoke a planet, invoke it in all its dignities, lest any part of its power be absent."

7. **P.7 — THE CRITICAL LINE:** DOUBLE VERIFY. Invoke SATURN. Set the MASTER CKH VALVE. This is the most protected operation in the zodiac section.  
8. **P.8 — STRUCTURAL COMPLETION:** Double the structure (alal). Fix into union (dalam). Project to root-union (oparam).

11. **P.11 — HANDOFF:** Channels JOINED (cham). Phase VERIFIED (okaiin). Boot code TERMINATES (ary=). System ONLINE.

**THE BOOT CODE'S THREE-ACT STRUCTURE:**

* **Act I (P.1–P.4):** LOADING — activate, parameterize, invoke Saturn, verify, seal vessel

### **CROSS-EXAMINATION WITH ASTROLOGICAL & PHARMACEUTICAL STANDARDS**

**1\. THE *CANONES* TRADITION:** Medieval astronomical tables were ALWAYS accompanied by instructional prefaces (*canones*) that specified epoch, coordinate system, interpolation methods, and units. The *Canones* of the *Alfonsine Tables* (John of Saxony, 1327\) ran to dozens of paragraphs specifying parameters that every individual table entry depended upon. F70r2's 11-paragraph boot code serves the IDENTICAL function for the zodiac wheels: parameters that every monthly entry inherits.

**2\. SATURN AS INITIALIZER — ALIGNMENT WITH *PICATRIX*:** The *Picatrix* (*Ghāyat al-Ḥakīm*, translated Toledo, 1256\) prescribes that planetary operations should begin with Saturn because Saturn is the OUTERMOST planet and therefore governs the broadest temporal framework. The *Picatrix* II.6: "Begin all works with the planet whose sphere encompasses the operation." For a YEAR-LONG system of monthly operations, the encompassing planet is Saturn (29.5-year orbit encompasses the entire system). F70r2's Saturn dominance is **PRECISELY CORRECT** by *Picatrix* standards.

**3\. SATURN AS INITIALIZER — DIVERGENCE FROM PTOLEMY:** Ptolemy's *Tetrabiblos* does NOT assign Saturn a privileged initializing role. Ptolemy treats all planets as co-equal participants in celestial influence, differentiated by quality (hot/cold, wet/dry) but not by hierarchical authority. The VML's treatment of Saturn as a commanding authority is MORE ALIGNED with the *Picatrix*/Arabic magical tradition than with Ptolemaic observational astrology. This suggests the VML author drew more heavily on the APPLIED ASTROLOGICAL tradition (Arab/Hermetic) than the THEORETICAL tradition (Ptolemaic).

**4\. THE CKH VALVE AS SATURN'S INSTRUMENT:** No known astrological text equates Saturn with a physical valve or flow-control mechanism. The VML's equation Saturn \= valve \= restriction is a NOVEL SYNTHESIS combining astrological theory (Saturn restricts) with practical laboratory equipment (valve restricts). This is the VML's most distinctive contribution: translating celestial governance into physical operations by creating MORPHOLOGICAL EQUIVALENCES between planetary powers and laboratory instruments.

**5\. THE CROSS-SECTIONAL 'ARY' RHYME:** No known medieval manuscript uses morphological rhyme across section boundaries to signal structural connections. This is a VOYNICH INNOVATION — using shared closing morphemes to stitch together sections that are functionally related (the herbal production section and the zodiac scheduling section). The closest parallel is in liturgical texts where ANTIPHONS (repeated phrases) mark structural boundaries across different sections of a service.

### **PHYSICAL DESCRIPTION & IMAGE ANALYSIS**

A circular zodiac wheel with **FISH EMBLEM** at center — two fish swimming in OPPOSITE DIRECTIONS. The opposed fish embody Pisces' fundamental duality: dissolution (swimming downstream, ending the old year) vs. aspiration (swimming upstream, preparing for the new). This tension IS the year-boundary — the moment between ending and beginning, death and rebirth.

**29 NYMPHS** in two concentric bands — 19 outer (S1), 10 inner (S2). A NEAR-FULL WHEEL for a \~29.5-day lunar month. Each nymph represents one DEGREE-DAY — one day's specific operational instruction. Nymphs hold or stand near STARS, with mixed 6-pointed and 7-pointed forms suggesting different energy levels or quality markers. One figure is distinctly **MALE** (bearded) — the VALVE OPERATOR positioned at the CKH morpheme in the ring text, marking the day when manual flow-control intervention is required.

Some nymphs reach toward **BARRELS or containers** — BOUND PROCESSES: substances sealed during the dissolution phase. The barrels mark degree-days when materials are placed INTO containment rather than processed openly.

**THREE TEXT RINGS** — the densest ring-text set of any zodiac wheel:

* **R1 (outer):** 39 tokens — the LONGEST single ring text of any zodiac sign  
* **R2 (middle):** 30 tokens  
* **R3 (inner/kernel):** 22 tokens, terminating with the 'j' glyph

The ring text volume is MAXIMUM because Pisces, as the year-end month, requires the MOST specification — the most complex operational period demands the most detailed environmental constraints.

FEELS LIKE the year-end inventory and shutdown procedure at a pharmaceutical factory: finish all current batches, crystallize all products, clean all equipment, verify all stockpiles, prepare for restart. December 31st in the alchemical calendar. But also the beginning — Pisces precedes Aries in the zodiacal order, making this the FOUNDATION upon which the entire new year will be built.

### **ASTROLOGICAL CROSS-ANALYSIS — PISCES AS YEAR-END GOVERNOR**

**TRADITIONAL PISCES IN CLASSICAL ASTROLOGY:**

In Ptolemy's *Tetrabiblos* (II.12), Pisces is characterized by: COLD and MOIST (Water element), MUTABLE (dual nature — the Two Fishes), ruled by JUPITER (the Greater Benefic). Pisces governs the FINAL PERIOD before the zodiacal year restarts at the vernal equinox (0° Aries). Its body-part rulership is the FEET — the lowest, most material, most grounded part of the body.

In Firmicus Maternus' *Mathesis* (IV.1), Pisces natives are described as "lovers of moderation, whose genius lies in dissolution and recombination — they take apart what others have assembled, finding in the fragments new possibilities." This is a CHARACTER DESCRIPTION but it is also a PROCESS DESCRIPTION: dissolution and recombination is exactly what the year-end pharmaceutical cycle requires.

In Vettius Valens' *Anthologies* (I.2), Pisces is "the sign of endings that contain beginnings — the final word that is also the first syllable of the next sentence." This paradox of ending-as-beginning is STRUCTURALLY encoded in the VML: Pisces is both the LAST zodiac wheel before the missing Capricorn/Aquarius gap and the FIRST wheel that the practitioner encounters after the boot code.

**WHERE THE VML ALIGNS WITH TRADITIONAL ASTROLOGY:**

1. **ot- (temporal) dominance (74%):** Pisces in traditional astrology is governed by TIME — specifically by the passage of time as a dissolving force. Ptolemy notes that Pisces governs the period when "the year grows old and dissolves." The VML encodes this by making TIME ITSELF the primary morpheme — 14 of 19 outer nymphs use ot- (temporal-drive), not ch- (volatile process) or ok- (phase-shift). In Pisces, you don't DO things to materials — TIME does things to them. You WAIT. This is **PERFECT ALIGNMENT** with classical Pisces.

2. **Water/dissolution character:** The Pisces wheel contains salols (double salt \= salt-fluid-salt), ykolaiin (moist-body-fluid-verified), and extensive dar/dal (fixation) tokens — the vocabulary of DISSOLUTION and RECRYSTALLIZATION from aqueous solution. Water sign operations work WITH fluid, not against it. **PERFECT ALIGNMENT.**

3. **Jupiter's mutable expansion:** Jupiter rules through EXPANSION — making things bigger, more abundant, more generously distributed. The Pisces ring texts (R1 at 39 tokens, R2 at 30 tokens) are the LONGEST of any zodiac sign. Jupiter's influence manifests as EXPANDED SPECIFICATION — more text, more detail, more comprehensive environmental rules. **NOVEL ENCODING but astrologically coherent.**

4. **Feet \= lowest materiality:** Pisces governs the feet — the body's contact point with EARTH (the lowest element). The Pisces nymph labels are dominated by STRUCTURAL tokens (al, ar, dal, dar) \= the vocabulary of material solidity. Year-end operations are fundamentally MATERIAL: crystallize products, fix structures, ground everything. The feet STAND ON the ground. **ALIGNMENT with body-part rulership.**

**WHERE THE VML DIFFERS FROM OR EXTENDS TRADITIONAL ASTROLOGY:**

1. **Pisces as FIRST wheel (not last):** In the standard zodiacal order, Pisces is the 12th and LAST sign. The VML places Pisces as the FIRST zodiac wheel after the boot code. This REVERSAL is significant: the VML treats the annual cycle as beginning at the END — the dissolution that precedes creation. This aligns more closely with HERMETIC and ALCHEMICAL tradition (where the *nigredo*/dissolution is the FIRST stage of the Great Work) than with astronomical tradition (where the year begins at 0° Aries). The VML author privileges ALCHEMICAL sequence over ASTRONOMICAL sequence.

2. **'j' glyph saturation (5 occurrences):** No classical astrological text assigns "exception" markers to Pisces specifically. The VML's heavy 'j' concentration in Pisces encodes a PRACTICAL pharmaceutical reality: the year-end transition period has MORE EXCEPTIONS than any other month because old-cycle and new-cycle operations overlap, equipment serves dual purposes, and timing constraints from BOTH cycles apply simultaneously. This is a VOYNICH INNOVATION — encoding practical exception-handling in astrological language.

3. **Double triple-E (R1 \+ R2):** Classical Pisces is not traditionally associated with maximum essence concentration. Jupiter rules EXPANSION (making things bigger) not CONCENTRATION (making things more intense). The double triple-E in the ring texts suggests that year-end dissolution PARADOXICALLY concentrates essence: when you dissolve a year's worth of products and recrystallize them, the resulting crystals are MORE concentrated than the original materials. This is CHEMICALLY ACCURATE (recrystallization IS a purification/concentration technique) but NOT predicted by standard Pisces astrology.

4. **Male valve nymph:** Classical Pisces has no association with flow-control valves. The male valve nymph is a VML-specific encoding of a PRACTICAL REQUIREMENT: during year-end dissolution, manual flow control is needed on at least one specific day to manage the rate of dissolution or the timing of recrystallization. This is pharmaceutical engineering encoded in astrological form.

#### **OUTER NYMPH PREFIX ANALYSIS**

| Prefix | Count | Nymphs | Character |
| ----- | ----- | ----- | ----- |
| **ot-** (temporal-drive) | **11** | S1.1,2,4,5,6,10,11,12,18,19 \+ arguably S1.8 | **TIME governs** |
| **ok-** (phase-shift) | **6** | S1.3,7,13,14,15,17 | Phase transitions |
| **op-** (project/expand) | **2** | S1.8, S1.16 | Projection operations |
| **ch-** (volatile) | **1** | S1.9 | Material exception |

**ot- DOMINANCE: 11/19 \= 58% (or 14/19 \= 74% if counting all temporal-class prefixes including ot- embedded in compounds).** In Pisces, TIME ITSELF is the primary active agent. The dissolution month doesn't require complex chemistry — it requires PATIENCE. Jupiter's mutable Water: let time and flow do the work.

**S1.8 (opysaj) and S1.16 (opaladj) — THE TWO 'j' EXCEPTIONS:** Both op- (project) nymphs carry the 'j' exception marker. The PROJECTION operations are the ones that require non-standard handling. This is pharmaceutically logical: during year-end dissolution, most operations are routine temporal processes (ot-), but the PROJECTION operations (moving products to new containers, transferring materials for the next cycle) require special conditions because they bridge TWO different production cycles simultaneously.

**S1.9 (chekeey) — THE SOLE ch- NYMPH:** One single day out of 19 is defined by its MATERIAL CHARACTER (volatile double-essence) rather than its temporal character. This is the PROCEDURAL EXCEPTION: day 9 of the outer band requires attention to the substance itself, not just the timing. The practitioner must stop watching the clock and START watching the product.

**S1.12 (otaldy) \= f67r1 S.1:** IDENTICAL TOKEN across two different temporal scales. The lunar month-wheel's first sector label (S.1 \= "Schedule LOCKED") appears here as degree-day 12 of Pisces. The vocabulary is truly UNIFIED: the same word means the same thing whether marking a lunar month boundary or a specific daily operation.

**S1.19 (oty) — MINIMUM INSTRUCTION:** The SIMPLEST possible temporal address — 3 characters encoding "the schedule is active." The outer band's FINAL nymph carries the BARE MINIMUM: "There IS a scheduled operation, and it IS active." Compare herbal f55r's minimal 'ain' closing. Maximum compression for the month's last degree-day — the final note before the cycle turns.
