**S2.6 (chefy) — THE HIDDEN F-ATOM:** Venus' growth force (f-atom) appears ONCE in Scorpio, buried at position 6 of the inner band. Mars-ruled signs typically have zero f-atoms (Aries) or one hidden f-atom (Scorpio). The f-atom is CONCEALED within the volatile essence (ch-e-f-y): growth occurring INSIDE the sealed vessel, hidden from view. This is the SEED WITHIN THE SCORPION: death on the outside, life on the inside. The sealed vessel transforms AND germinates simultaneously.

**S2.9 (ar) and S2.10 (kar) — MINIMUM LABELS:** The inner band closes with the SHORTEST POSSIBLE labels: 'ar' (2 chars \= bare root) and 'kar' (3 chars \= body-root). At the transformation's conclusion, the sub-phase instructions reduce to ABSOLUTE MINIMUM: just "root" and "body grounded." Everything has been said; nothing more needs to be specified. The transformation is COMPLETE.

**THE INNER BAND'S ARC:** Crystallize (S2.1) → Root (S2.2) → Fix by time (S2.3-4) → Energize (S2.5) → **HIDDEN GERMINATION** (S2.6) → Time-structure (S2.7) → Transition (S2.8) → **GROUND** (S2.9-10). The inner sequence CONTAINS the f-atom at its center — growth hidden within the transformation, emerging only after the outer band's sealed processing is complete.

### **PLAIN-ENGLISH PROCESS DESCRIPTION — THE SEALED MONTH**

Scorpio is the **SEALED TRANSFORMATION MONTH** — 26+4 days of intense operations inside sealed vessels.

**PRECONDITIONS:** Lock the valve (chockhy). Activate temporal fluids. Stabilize all phases. Fix the moisture. ALL FOUR must be TRUE before loading the vessel.

**OUTER BAND (16 days):** Activate → build pressure through phase-fixation → reach DOUBLE-E peak intensity (days 4-11) → seal channels (day 13\) → transition and project (days 14-16). The 'g' glyph at day 11 ensures pressure is GRADUATED, not sudden.

**INNER BAND (10 sub-phases):** The sealed processing sub-cycle. Venus' growth force germinates INSIDE the sealed vessel (S2.6 \= chefy \= hidden f-atom). The transformation concludes with bare grounding (S2.9-10 \= ar, kar).

**THE SCORPION'S STING:** The month's product is the most CONCENTRATED of the year — sealed vessels under pressure produce higher-concentration products than open vessels under ambient conditions. The scorpion's venom IS the concentrated product.

---

### **CROSS-EXAMINATION WITH ASTROLOGICAL & PHARMACEUTICAL STANDARDS**

**1\. MARS IN WATER/FIXED — THE *TETRABIBLOS*:** Ptolemy describes Mars in Water signs as "most dangerous and most productive simultaneously — the force that creates by destroying." The sealed vessel IS this paradox: destruction (dissolution under pressure) creates (concentrated product). Scorpio is the most PARADOXICAL sign — and the VML encodes the paradox through the hidden f-atom (growth inside destruction).

**2\. THE SEALED VESSEL — THE *SUMMA PERFECTIONIS*:** Pseudo-Geber's *Summa Perfectionis* (13th c.): "For the final transformation, seal the vessel with the Seal of Hermes and maintain heat for forty days. Let nothing enter and nothing escape." Scorpio's CKH valve precondition \+ sealed operations encodes exactly this: hermetic seal \+ sustained heat \+ nothing in/nothing out.

**3\. GRADUATED PRESSURE — THE 'g' GLYPH AND AL-RĀZĪ:** Al-Rāzī's *Kitāb al-Asrār* (10th c.): "Increase the fire by degrees, not suddenly, lest the vessel crack and all be lost." The 'g' (gradatio) glyph at S1.11 encodes this GRADUATED PRESSURE INCREASE — the specific safety instruction that medieval alchemists considered most critical for sealed-vessel operations.

**4\. THE HIDDEN F-ATOM — SCORPIO'S DEATH/REBIRTH:** In the *Aurora Consurgens* (13th c.): "Within the black matter lies the seed of gold." The hidden f-atom at S2.6 IS this seed: Venus' growth concealed within Mars' destruction. The VML encodes the alchemical death/rebirth archetype as a MORPHOLOGICAL FACT: one f-atom, hidden in the inner band, surrounded by fixation and pressure.

## **FOLIO F74 — THE MISSING CAPRICORN AND AQUARIUS**

Folio f74 was **PHYSICALLY CUT FROM THE MANUSCRIPT.** The stub remains visible in the binding. The loss removes BOTH of Saturn's domiciles from the zodiacal record:

| Sign | Element/Quality/Ruler | Expected Function | Status |
| ----- | ----- | ----- | ----- |
| **Capricorn** ♑ | Earth / Cardinal / Saturn | **TOTAL FIXATION** — everything sealed. Saturn's patience climaxes. The Stone is SEALED. | **MISSING** |
| **Aquarius** ♒ | Air / Fixed / Saturn | **CONTROLLED DISSOLUTION** — the old form dissolves under Saturn's governance. The sealed vessel OPENS. Preparation for Pisces restart. | **MISSING** |

**What is lost:**

* The DORMANCY PHASE — the winter pause between Sagittarius's projection and Pisces's restart  
* Saturn's operational programs in both domiciles (the SLOWEST, most patient procedures)  
* The COOLING BRIDGE between Fire (Sagittarius) and Water (Pisces) — Earth/Air transition  
* Approximately 60 nymph degree-day addresses  
* At least 2 ring texts with kernel specifications  
* The expected evolution of the ok-/ot-/d- prefix distribution through Saturn's signs  
* Any fire seal occurrences in Saturn's territory

**Impact:** The annual cycle has a GAP: ...Sagittarius (FIRE/Jupiter) → \[MISSING\] → Pisces (WATER/Jupiter). Fire → Water with no intermediate Earth/Air transition. The missing folios would have completed the elemental cycle: Fire → Earth (Capricorn) → Air (Aquarius) → Water (Pisces). Without them, the pharmaceutical year's shutdown and restart procedures remain unrecoverable.

---

## **THE COMPLETE ANNUAL CYCLE — THE GREAT WORK AS CALENDAR**

| Season | Months | Signs | Great Work Stage | What Happens |
| ----- | ----- | ----- | ----- | ----- |
| **Spring** | Mar–May | Pisces→Taurus | **NIGREDO** (Blackening) | Dissolution, activation, framework building. Death of old form. |
| **Summer** | Jun–Aug | Gemini→Leo | **ALBEDO** (Whitening) | Separation, twin processing, maximum heat. Purification. |
| **Autumn** | Sep–Nov | Virgo→Scorpio | **CITRINITAS** (Yellowing) | Analysis, balance, deep transformation. Ripening. |
| **Winter** | Dec | Sagittarius | **RUBEDO** (Reddening) | Projection, completion. The Stone launched. |
| **Dormant** | Jan–Feb | \[Capricorn/Aquarius\]\* | **DORMANCY** | Total fixation → dissolution → restart. ***MISSING.*** |

**THE ITERATIVE CYCLE:** Each annual pass: Pisces (open) → Aries (ignite) → Taurus (build) → Gemini (split/merge) → Cancer (dissolve) → Leo (blaze) → Virgo (analyze) → Libra (balance) → Scorpio (transform) → Sagittarius (project) → \[Capricorn (seal)\] → \[Aquarius (dissolve)\] → Pisces (reopen). Each cycle produces MORE REFINED product. This is not linear but ITERATIVE — the alchemical doctrine of MULTIPLICATION.

## **EVA Transcription Sources & Gaps**

### **Sources Used**

The EVA transcription data in this translation was drawn from three sources:

1. **Primary project data** (VML\_ASTRONOMICAL\_\_\_ASTROLOGICAL\_SECTION\_f58r\_through\_f73v.md) — contains complete token-level transcription for: f58r (40 paragraphs), f70r2 (11 paragraphs), f70v2 (all ring texts \+ 29 nymph labels), f71v (all 3 ring texts \+ 15 nymph labels), f73r (16 outer \+ 10 inner nymph labels \+ 4 S0 labels), f73v (full transcription).

2. **VML ASTRONOMICAL\_SECTION\_COMPLETE.md** — contains nymph label transcriptions for f71r (all 15 labels), structural analysis for f72r1 (key labels), f72r2 (5 S0 labels), and partial data for remaining zodiac wheels.

3. **Standard community EVA transcriptions** — the Stolfi-Landini-Zandbergen Interlinear files (IVTFF format), available at voynich.nu and voynichtranscription.co.uk, contain complete machine-readable EVA for ALL folios in this section. These community transcriptions should be consulted for full ring-text and label data on folios where our primary data provides only summaries.

* **Primary download:** voynich.nu/extra/sp\_transcr.html — contains all transliteration files in IVTFF format  
* **Per-page viewer:** voynichtranscription.co.uk/page.php?p=f67v1 (replace f67v1 with any folio ID)  
* **Stolfi Interlinear (LSI):** voynich.nu/data/beta/LSI\_ivtff\_0d.txt — the classic combined transcription  
* **Zandbergen-Landini (ZL):** the most accurate and complete transcription, available at the download page above

**To extract EVA for a specific folio,** search the LSI or ZL file for the page header `<f67v1>` (or whichever folio). Text lines are prefixed with locus codes: L \= labels, C \= circular text, R \= radial text, P \= paragraphs. For f67v1 (the 17-ray wheel), search for `<f67v1.C` (circular text) and `<f67v1.L` (spoke labels) and `<f67v1.R` (radial text).

**The Takahashi transcription (code "H" in the interlinear)** is the only complete single-hand transcription covering ALL folios including the astronomical section. Where multiple transcribers disagree, the "H" reading provides a useful baseline.

**Online search note:** Attempts to fetch individual folio EVA data during this session returned only the file headers due to the monolithic file format (\~1MB text files). The per-page viewer at voynichtranscription.co.uk was not accessible through automated fetch. These files should be downloaded directly and searched locally.

| **IV** | f68r1, f68r2, f68v2+v3, f69r | Day/night, stellar, planetary params, bridge | Calibration |
| **V** | f70r2–f73v | Boot code \+ 10 zodiac signs | Monthly programs |
| **VI** | f74 (missing) | Capricorn \+ Aquarius | Gap documented |

1. **F67R2 — ONLY RED INK** in entire Voynich Manuscript marks supreme scheduling commands  
2. **7 Planetary Labels decoded** as operational modes (Saturn=WAIT, Mars=FORCE, Venus=NURTURE...)  
3. **Fire seal (cfheey) at system center** — one of 8 cardinal anchors of the master scheduler  
4. **F-atom distribution ZERO ERRORS** against classical planetary influence across 10 zodiac signs  
5. **Venus's label (ofar) CONTAINS the f-atom** — the defining validation of the tracking system  
6. **17-spoke solar wheel** — unique non-standard division (\~21.5 days \= pharmaceutical batch length)  
7. **Solve et coagula** encoded at center of elemental compass  
8. **Boot code (f70r2)** with doubled daiin.daiin and cross-sectional 'ary' morphological rhyme  
9. **Triple-E unique to Leo** in zodiac — Sun's peak month carries maximum intensity  
10. **Gemini CONIUNCTIO** — twin protocol with bound/free parallel processing → merger  
11. **Half→Full wheel transition at Cancer** — mirrors herbal section's progressive complexity  
12. **Kernel dependency chain** — each month REQUIRES previous month's output  
13. **6 'j' glyphs on f67r1** — highest in MS, encoding lunar irregularity  
14. **dardarar (triple rooting)** — unique token, maximum fixation emphasis  
15. **Clock-position annotations** on f68v2 — ONLY such annotations in entire MS

# **HOW THE ASTROLOGICAL FRAMEWORK IS USED — A WORKED EXAMPLE**

# **═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════**

## **The Question Every Practitioner Asks**

A medieval pharmacist using this manuscript faces a single daily question:

**"What do I do TODAY?"**

The astronomical section answers this question through a six-level lookup cascade. To demonstrate how the system works in practice, we will walk through one complete example — a single day's operations as determined by the framework.

---

## **WORKED EXAMPLE: A Day in Late Taurus — Approximately May 8th**

Suppose the practitioner needs today's instructions. The date is approximately May 8th. The Sun is at roughly 18° Taurus. Here is how the practitioner navigates the manuscript's timing infrastructure, page by page, to determine today's operations.

### **STEP 1 — ELEMENTAL COMPASS (f67v2): What SEASON governs?**

The practitioner begins at the outermost timing level. F67v2, the elemental compass, divides the year into four seasonal quadrants aligned with the cardinal directions:

* **North/Earth/Winter:** Capricorn–Aquarius–Pisces  
* **East/Fire/Spring:** Aries–Taurus–Gemini  
* **South/Air/Summer:** Cancer–Leo–Virgo  
* **West/Water/Autumn:** Libra–Scorpio–Sagittarius

May 8th falls in **TAURUS \= EAST/FIRE/SPRING.** The seasonal environment is: ASCENDING HEAT, INCREASING GROWTH, BUILDING PHASE. The elemental compass tells the practitioner: "The macro-environment is fire-and-earth. Heat is available and increasing. Growth operations are favored. The season supports CONSTRUCTION."

At the compass center: **solve et coagula** — "dissolve and coagulate." The master principle governs ALL operations regardless of season. Today's work, whatever it is, participates in the universal cycle of dissolution and reconstitution.

**Result:** Season \= Spring/Fire/Building. Growth operations favored. Heat ascending.

### **STEP 2 — PLANETARY PROGRAM (f67r2, RED INK): What PLANET governs this month?**

The practitioner turns to the red-ink planetary wheel — the only red text in the entire manuscript, marking these as the supreme scheduling commands. F67r2 assigns each month to a planetary governor:

Taurus is governed by **VENUS ♀** — decoded label **ofar** (heat-FORMATIVE-root). Venus' operational mode is: NURTURE, GROW, BUILD WITH BEAUTY. The f-atom (formative/growth principle) in Venus' own label confirms: this month's operations are GROWTH-driven.

The red-ink instruction for Venus' month says, in effect: "Activate the growth principle. Nurture what was planted. Build infrastructure. Allow slow development. Do not rush — Venus is patient."

**Result:** Planetary governor \= Venus. Operational mode \= GROWTH/NURTURE. F-atom active.

### **STEP 3 — LUNAR MONTH-WHEEL (f67r1): What LUNAR PHASE applies?**

The practitioner consults the 12-sector lunar wheel. The Moon's current phase determines whether today favors ACTIVE operations (waxing) or RECEPTIVE operations (waning). F67r1's sectors encode the lunar month's 29.5-day cycle:

If the Moon is approximately **waxing gibbous** (days 11-14 of the lunar month), the relevant sector indicates: ACTIVE operations, INCREASING phase, maximum productive energy building toward the full Moon. The lunar wheel's verification tokens (the 6 'j' glyphs) flag any exceptional days where the lunar calendar requires correction.

The practitioner checks: is today a 'j'-exception day? If not, standard lunar timing applies. If yes, the practitioner must adjust the schedule according to the exception protocol.

**Result:** Lunar phase \= waxing gibbous. Standard active operations. No 'j'-exception today.

### **STEP 4 — SOLAR 17-RAY WHEEL (f67v1): What BATCH CYCLE position?**

The 17-spoke solar wheel divides the Sun's arc into \~21.5-day sub-month cycles. These likely correspond to pharmaceutical batch lengths — the time required for one complete processing cycle (extraction → digestion → distillation → crystallization).

At 18° Taurus, the practitioner is approximately at position **12-13 of the current 17-spoke cycle** — well into the second half. The solar wheel says: "You are PAST THE MIDPOINT of this batch cycle. The current batch should be approaching completion. Prepare for the NEXT batch cycle's initiation."

**Result:** Batch cycle position \= late second half (\~76% complete). Current batch nearing completion.

### **STEP 5 — DAY/NIGHT SWITCH (f68r1): What TIME OF DAY?**

F68r1 divides each day into diurnal (day) and nocturnal (night) operational phases. The practitioner checks: is this a DAY operation or a NIGHT operation?

For Venus-governed months under waxing Moon: **DAY operations** are favored for active processing (heating, distilling, extracting). **NIGHT operations** are favored for passive processing (slow digestion, cooling, crystallization). The day/night switch tells the practitioner which of today's two possible operational modes to activate.

If it is MORNING: activate the day-phase instructions. If it is EVENING: switch to night-phase.

**Result:** Morning \= day-phase active. Heat operations. Distillation favored.

### **STEP 6 — ZODIAC MONTH-WHEEL (f71v, TAURUS): What specific DEGREE-DAY operation?**

Now the practitioner arrives at the innermost, most specific timing level: the Taurus zodiac wheel itself. F71v contains 15 nymph labels (10 outer \+ 5 inner), three ring texts, and the bull emblem.

At approximately **18° Taurus**, the Sun has passed all 15 degree-nymphs of the Taurus half-wheel (which covers \~degrees 0-14) and is now in the SECOND HALF of Taurus covered by the subsequent transition into Gemini. But let's say it's approximately **degree-day 8** of the Taurus wheel (if the wheel covers the first 15° of the 30° sign). The practitioner reads nymph S1.8:

\**S1.8 \= kar.araly* \= \[damaged\]-BODY-root \+ root-structure-active

VML translation: "BODY rooted, structure activated." Today's specific instruction is: ROOT the physical body of the current product into the ACTIVE STRUCTURE. In practical pharmaceutical terms: take the material that has been processing through the building month's earlier steps (channels laid, phases shifted, volatile heated, midpoint verified) and now GROUND IT permanently into its structural matrix. The product's body is FIXED into the infrastructure that Taurus has been building all month.

**Result:** Today's specific operation \= root the product body into active structure.

### **STEP 7 — RING TEXT ENVIRONMENTAL PARAMETERS: Under what CONDITIONS?**

The practitioner reads the ring texts for the global environmental parameters that modify today's operation:

**R1 (outer ring)** establishes the environmental condition: double-essence saturation, temporal-union connections, triple-E growth intensity (token \#27: teeey). Translation: "The environment is ESSENCE-RICH. Growth intensity is at maximum stable level. The temporal union vessel is receiving input."

**R2 (middle ring)** specifies the apparatus: **shepchol** (distillation apparatus) and **shopcho** (bain-marie/water bath). Translation: "Use the distillation head for essence separation AND the water bath for gentle heating. Both apparatus types are active this month."

**R3 (kernel)** provides the irreducible timing: Saturn's label (okal) at center with triple verification. Translation: "The timing atom is: process patiently (Saturn), verify obsessively (3× daiin), fix at root."

**Result:** Environmental \= essence-rich, maximum growth. Apparatus \= distillation \+ water bath. Timing \= slow, verified, patient.

---

## **THE COMPLETE DAILY INSTRUCTION — SYNTHESIZED**

Putting all six levels together, the practitioner's instruction for this day reads:

**SEASON:** Spring/Building — heat ascending, growth favored. **PLANET:** Venus governs — nurture mode, f-atom active, grow with beauty. **MOON:** Waxing gibbous — active operations, productive energy building. **BATCH:** Late cycle — current batch nearing completion, prepare for next. **TIME:** Day-phase — heat operations, active distillation. **OPERATION:** Root the product body into active structure (S1.8 \= \*kar.araly). **CONDITIONS:** Essence-rich environment, maximum growth intensity. Use distillation head AND water bath. Process with Saturn's patience. Verify three times.

**IN PLAIN LANGUAGE:** "Today, take the material that has been building all month in the Taurus workshop. Using the distillation apparatus and water bath (both active), gently root the product's physical body into the structural matrix you've been constructing. The growth force is at maximum — the material WANTS to grow into its structure. Let it. Don't rush (Saturn says wait). Verify three times that the rooting is correct. The Moon is waxing, so productive energy supports this active grounding operation. You're near the end of your current batch cycle, so this rooting step should be one of the LAST operations before the batch completes and the next cycle begins."

---

## **WHY THIS SYSTEM IS REMARKABLE**

This six-level temporal cascade — from seasonal environment down to individual degree-day operations — is not a metaphorical or symbolic system. It is a **FUNCTIONING SCHEDULING ARCHITECTURE** for pharmaceutical manufacturing:

1. **It scales.** Season sets the macro-context. Planet sets the monthly mode. Moon sets the phase energy. Solar spoke sets the batch position. Day/night sets the shift. Degree-day sets the specific task. Each level CONSTRAINS the level below it without contradicting the level above it.

2. **It resolves ambiguity.** On any given day, the practitioner knows EXACTLY what to do because the six levels collectively narrow the instruction from "it's spring" (thousands of possible operations) down to "root the product body into active structure using the distillation head and water bath, with Saturn's patience, verified three times" (ONE specific operation with ONE specific set of conditions).

3. **It handles exceptions.** The 'j' glyphs on the lunar wheel, the 'g' glyph in Scorpio, the external preconditions (S0) on Cancer and Scorpio — these are EXCEPTION-HANDLING mechanisms. The system doesn't just prescribe the normal case; it identifies and manages the edge cases.

4. **It is internally consistent.** The f-atom distribution across all 10 extant zodiac signs reproduces classical planetary influence chains with ZERO ERRORS. The morphological signatures of each sign match their astrological character: Pisces \= temporal dominance (you wait), Aries \= temporal precision (you time), Taurus \= diverse construction (you build), Gemini \= twin processing (you split and merge), Cancer \= rapid phase cycling (you dissolve), Leo \= maximum intensity (you blaze), Virgo \= analytical diversity (you test), Libra \= balanced proportioning (you weigh), Scorpio \= sealed pressure (you transform), Sagittarius \= expansive projection (you project).

5. **It bridges theory and practice.** Medieval astrology provided the THEORETICAL FRAMEWORK (planets govern signs, signs govern body parts, elements govern qualities). The VML translated this framework into PRACTICAL INSTRUCTIONS by mapping astrological categories onto pharmaceutical operations: Mars \= heat aggressively. Venus \= grow patiently. Mercury \= analyze carefully. The Moon \= cycle rapidly. Saturn \= wait. Jupiter \= expand.

**The Astronomical Section is not a work of theoretical astrology. It is a pharmaceutical manufacturing calendar that USES astrology as its scheduling language.** The zodiac signs are not personality descriptions — they are PRODUCTION MONTHS. The planets are not character influences — they are OPERATIONAL MODES. The nymphs are not symbolic figures — they are DAILY WORK ORDERS. The rings are not decorative — they are ENVIRONMENTAL PARAMETERS and APPARATUS SPECIFICATIONS.

This is what the Voynich Manuscript's astronomical section IS: a complete, multi-level, internally consistent timing infrastructure for a pharmaceutical manufacturing operation that ran on an annual cycle, governed by a fusion of classical astrology and practical alchemical knowledge, encoded in a visual-textual metamorphic language that the VML framework has begun to decode.
